2c\x03\x18\x6f\xdd\x73\xc6\x75\xcb\x42\x20\x20\x11\x11\x9b\xd8\x4a\xca\x0d\xa9\x1d\xe1\xcf\xdb\x14\x19\x12\xac\x80\x0b\x9e\x92\x17\x8d\x4a\xc7\xe9\xf1\x52\xcf\x7b\x98\x0e\xe0\x74\x65\x15\xe3\x98\xc2\x7f\xd3\x5d\x09\x24\x26\x71\x2f\xa0\x76\x85\x85\xa6\x64\x05\x82\xf8\xb3\xf2\xdc\xde\x8d\xf8\xfa\x0b\x19\x1e\x14\x24\x56\x37\xc3\xad\xcc\x8d\x38\xbb\x0e\x3c\x90\xea\x31\xf8\xb6\xb1\x0b\x84\xa6\x02\x67\x71\x8a\xb9\x71\x19\x2d\x94\x1a\xb6\xa8\xf9\x43\x4d\x0c\x3b\xb8\xdb\xf0\xbb\x19\x34\xb2\xff\x07\xc1\x42\x21\xad\x7b\xdb\xe7\x24\x20\xe6\xbb\xbb\xb1\xe0\x6f\xe2\xe1\x3b\xc1\x2d\xb7\x56\x23\xde\xc8\xb4\x5c\x95\xb1\xec\x99\xab\x39\x84\x63\x47\xe4\x8b\xd1\x2a\x48\x53\x8e\x08\x72\xf8\x52\xc4\x7e\xc1\xb1\xa0\xb5\x6f\x65\x7a\x41\x9d\x9f\x67\x8e\xe2\x75\xed\x9c\x6b\x90\xb3\x7d\x06\xe6\xbd\x79\x0a\x9f\x63\xcf\x61\xc4\x47\x48\xf4\x64\x17\x05\xb6\x5f\x58\x39\xde\xfd\xd0\x1b\x6d\xa3\x5a\x89\xc4\x66\xe1\x4d\xbd\xbc\xd8\xbd\xdf\x3c\x49\x25\x30\x78\xb3\x20\x6e\x14\x03\xee\x31\xf3\x0f\x22\x7e\x5e\xb1\x94\x3f\x4a\x09\x58\x44\xb0\xcc\xf9\xea\x6e\x67\x67\x89\x24\xa9\x7c\x7f\xfd\xfd\xf6\x88\xea\xdd\x66\x9e\xaa\x0b\x71\xc4\x62\xda\x12\x60\x3e\x71\xf3\x40\x5a\x90\x04\x69\x65\xfc\x01\x16\x20\x5e\xb1\xae\xaf\x89\x64\x84\x94\xc1\xb4\x6a\xb1\x49\xbe\xf1\x08\xb5\x8c\x3a\x45\x2d\x8d\x68\x5d\x90\x73\x70\x44\xc4\xce\x4f\x61\xff\xbb\x21\xbb\xf6\x82\x2d\x58\x67\x15\x60\xbc\x74\x9d\x00\xbe\xca\x70\x9d\x1c\x7d\x8d\xd8\x5d\xff\x8d\x20\xe5\x13\x49\x17\x6d\x84\x5e\xde\x98\x8d\xef\xe7\x4e\x83\xf1\xaf\xd5\x04\x4d\x9e\x20\xdf\x54\x48\x3b\xc1\xc5\x38\xb4\xbd\x5e\x13\xa4\xb1\xbb\x2f\x68\x08\x95\xc9\x55\x29\xa2\xb3\x9d\x73\x94\xb9\x5d\x25\xe7\xe4\x0c\xbc\x41\x7f\x8d\x76\x05\x26\x2e\x1e\x05\x3d\x97\x8e\x14\x00\x81\x66\x7c\x87\x58\x2a\xdf\x46\x0c\x16\x36\xb4\x9b\x20\xc3\xed\x54\x70\x8d\xa7\xab\x59\x59\xd1\x4e\x1e\xe9\x94\x01\x99\xd7\x87\xd5\xfb\x93\x5d\xec\x8c\x0d\x7b\xb0\x3f\xac\xab\xad\xfb\x6e\xec\x45\xa1\xdb\x13\x42\xc7\x2b\xf4\xab\xc0\x11\x88\xeb\x85\x31\x91\xa7\x29\xb6\xc5\x90\x40\x8d\x8d\x27\xee\x50\x6a\x16\x7f\x16\xc2\x6e\x75\xd8\x5c\x04\x12\xbd\x45\x07\x38\x3b\x26\x64\x49\x42\x5c\x6d\x29\x81\x4f\xde\x6a\x68\x19\xe2\x2a\xd9\x80\xc1\xe6\xfa\x23\x1c\x3a\x7b\xcf\x5c\x12\x8f\x7b\x6d\x66\x00\x91\xe6\xa1\x73\x5c\xee\x9d\xc7\xfa\xb8\x45\xec\xd8\x52\xee\xd4\x12\x12\xc8\xb3\xbd\xd8\x27\x7f\xed\x48\x62\xf7\xd5\x6e\x1c\x3b\x1e\xdb\x78\x8e\x8a\xa8\x7e\xcb\xd0\xda\xa2\x8f\x2f\x4f\x7e\x84\x14\x9a\xec\x32\x0c\x95\x43\xf8\x55\xa3\x12\x5f\x39\x28\x44\x59\x67\x5a\xdb\x09\xf4\x5c\xc5\x52\x27\x0f\xa4\x20\x05\x6c\x11\x80\x0f\x11\x27\xb5\x85\x39\x74\x27\x77\xc3\x44\x37\x88\x80\xbe\x8b\xbc\x92\xc2\xcd\xfd\xc1\x2f\x4a\x43\x4f\xf5\xad\xcc\x1f\x1f\x9f\x0b\xdb\x51\xc2\xa2\x85\x2c\x1e\x80\xda\xc0\x16\x71\xff\xb8\x36\x90\x57\xf2\xf1\xf1\x4c\xa6\xba\x3a\xce\x22\x5c\x50\xd0\xf2\x15\x62\xcf\xec\x18\xd9\x96\xa7\xd6\xd0\x44\xca\x7b\xc5\x56\x50\x55\xf1\x67\x00\x37\xf8\xe8\xee\x5e\x2b\xbd\x7a\x8a\x6a\xd3\xcf\x48\x49\xb8\xcc\x6f\xc6\xf0\x47\x3f\x9f\x59\x1d\xc0\x4b\x5d\x23\x43\x11\x47\xa5\xf3\x3c\x96\xc4\x2f\x5d\x98\xe1\x7e\x7a\x52\xbc\x36\xa8\x86\x9b\x58\xf2\x8f\x34\xd8\x2b\xbb\xd7\xc0\x3b\x47\x29\xf2\xcd\xe3\xd5\x81\xd4\x12\xb2\xb8\xb1\xe2\x68\xf8\x46\xf8\x2c\xd2\x1b\xc9\xb1\x07\x01\x29\x59\xb8\xb4\xf5\xab\xd5\x67\x49\xb5\x23\xac\x7b\x97\x9b\xbe\x04\xcb\x35\x40\xbd\xdc\x9f\x2e\x21\xd4\xa7\x41\x0a\x7c\xf5\xe0\xe5\x9c\x52\x7d\xeb\xaa\x02\x55\x1f\x30\x3e\x07\x21\xd0\xcd\xc4\xa9\xcb\x5d\x3d\x54\x79\x82\xcf\x79\xf2\x74\xf1\x1d\xb6\x66\xd9\x59\x38\x52\xc8\x37\x57\x87\x38\x9d\x7b\x03\x8f\xf7\x9c\x35\x87\xe8\x98\x44\xc3\x51\x45\xeb\xdf\x45\xde\x74\x4b\x2f\xf4\x4e\xd9\x5a\x3d\x06\x4a\x97\x21\x66\x48\x63\xa1\x0f\xb3\x4b\xcd\x3f\x43\x94\xb1\x91\xd5\xca\x03\x03\x75\x83\xbe\x66\x3b\xd9\xfd\xe1\x91\x64\xaa\xe4\xa8\xfd\xbf\xcc\x2d\x2f\x6c\x8a\x48\xec\xd9\xbe\x03\x45\xda\x5f\x3f\x32\xef\x9d\x9d\x0a\x91\x16\x51\xe1\x2c\xe0\x20\x3b\x39\x8f\x2d\xe1\x71\x10\xa3\x5b\x14\x87\x21\x69\x5d\xc8\x90\x93\x04\x7f\x89\x8a\xfd\x35\x81\x18\xbd\x9b\x86\x7e\x24\x84\x89\x16\x34\x04\x4e\xb1\x78\x4f\xb6\x6a\xa6\x3d\x83\x30\xc1\xc7\x4c\x68\x52\xa0\xf8\x98\x19\xe7\xa5\x06\x4e\xd5\xe6\x61\x3d\x30\xd7\x58\x5d\x7a\x09\x20\x04\x95\x2f\x80\x2a\xb9\x1d\xfb\xc1\x69\x6f\x01\x4c\x99\x78\x23\xc5\x5f\x6d\xa0\x32\x87\x7b\x3e\x79\x78\xc3\x54\x52\x27\x19\xca\x63\xb7\x89\x4c\x50\xb6\x00\xdf\x24\x8b\xc7\x98\x58\x79\x21\xe2\xa3\x74\x2a\x3b\xc0\x8a\x19\x8e\xbd\x9f\x22\xc8\x4f\x64\x73\x7d\xc9\x11\x86\x8a\x20\x16\x38\xff\x7e\x23\x8a\xf0\xd9\x4a\x37\x0b\xc2\x84\xe5\x5e\x0b\xba\xed\xec\x33\x5a\xa5\xb5\x49\xc6\xbc\x4a\x00\x69\xf2\xb1\x4f\x2c\x9a\x18\x3e\xd4\x99\x7f\xd8\x5c\x61\x58\xcf\x35\x71\x59\xac\x89\x46\x07\xf1\x60\x30\x44\xb8\x06\xdd\x09\x37\xad\xa4\x1a\x5b\x93\x46\xce\x55\xfc\x21\xc1\x86\x98\xcc\x65\x2b\xbf\x77\x72\x4a\x2d\xd3\x1d\x52\x4b\xff\x3a\x3f\x02\x81\x48\xcd\x94\x7b\xb1\x2a\x9c\xc2\x0e\xf2\xe4\x22\xaf\xed\xec\x5a\x5a\xa5\x05\x31\x85\x52\x0d\x4d\x20\x36\x2d\x3b\xef\x09\x11\x93\x7d\xa6\x4d\x6b\x4d\x7e\x9a\x3e\x52\x89\x44\x87\xab\xba\xc9\xcf\x8b\xb8\x12\x92\xad\xcb\xf1\x2b\xb1\x1e\x7a\x0e\x8d\x0c\x0d\x1b\x33\xc8\xa1\x30\xf6\x84\xee\x1b\x81\x18\x22\x8b\x4d\xb6\x2f\xfe\xd1\xb1\xaf\x39\x17\xd4\x68\x1d\x56\xcc\xaa\x67\xb7\xea\x92\x17\xb1\x3b\x59\x81\xd6\x4c\x20\x21\x51\xc6\x48\xc4\x52\xab\x91\x08\x68\xa6\xa0\x79\x11\x73\x5d\xc7\xda\xa3\x2f\x10\xac\xa7\xf5\x91\x9d\xb8\xbd\xc8\x81\xd2\x7e\xcc\x25\xd6\x21\x34\x3c\x76\x78\xa1\xe4\x80\x50\xe0\x94\xe1\x18\xa9\x09\xd9\x5c\xc2\x5d\x8e\xee\xa1\xc5\x33\x26\xec\x39\x39\xc6\xb8\x1c\xb6\x71\x32\xaf\x2d\x9a\x12\x84\xf7\xb5\xd9\xca\xf2\xf5\xe4\x88\x87\x44\x1b\xdc\xa3\x71\x2d\x5f\xe4\x74\x15\x57\x92\x4d\xb9\x25\xb1\x82\xc5\x14\xd8\xcb\x71\xe0\x5b\x05\x86\x26\x54\x6b\x1f\xc2\x6e\xf5\x68\xf4\x10\xb3\x3b\xb0\x2a\xba\x21\x45\x01\x71\x92\xd7\xb6\x46\x29\x0c\xdc\x34\xce\xc6\x8c\x7e\x43\x5e\xef\x20\x2b\x80\x59\x63\x70\x06\x50\x2a\x00\x8f\xa2\x0b\x0c\x83\x90\x1e\xc6\xd7\x05\x70\xd5\xec\xe0\x32\x5a\x98\x5b\x94\x34\x23\x58\x08\x39\x21\xda\xba\xdb\xe0\xc7\x72\x17\x51\xe2\x3b\x5e\xe1\x18\xc6\xd1\x9a\x8d\xe5\x4f\x34\x41\x49\x15\x4a\xfc\x51\xb7\x71\x7c\xcd\x20\x1f\x2d\x33\xd9\x68\x0b\x64\x58\x52\x7b\x 18\x9d\xf2\x66\x37\x26\x85\x44\xf1\x80\xf5\x9c\x5e\x9b\x5e\x9a\x47\x09\xda\x46\xc0\x7a\x1c\x1e\x72\x64\xe0\x10\xa8\x52\x1d\xed\x39\xb2\x89\xbb\x22\x41\xeb\x34\x9b\xcb\x37\xb9\x93\xda\xe0\x38\x27\xd0\x6e\xe6\x92\x4e\x84\xe2\xd7\x17\x2e\xb6\xe1\x30\xae\x6e\x5f\x85\x5e\x09\xc8\x48\xef\x9e\xc1\x83\x88\x32\xe5\x1a\xbf\xb5\x45\x9e\x7b\xbb\xcf\xe1\xcd\xef\xad\x08\xfe\x40\x94\x5e\x1a\x51\x37\xb0\x63\x6e\x18\xa3\x7c\x24\x61\x1b\x52\xed\x46\x9b\xb9\x7c\x7f\x65\x5b\x23\xaa\x0d\x7a\xe8\x8f\x05\xe4\x6a\x2d\x47\x34\x10\x83\x7d\x31\x3f\x34\xc3\xac\x64\x57\xfd\x01\x47\x21\x87\xca\x1b\x90\x4a\x6b\xc4\xce\x45\x80\x3a\x3e\x9d\x54\xa7\xbd\x2b\x13\xef\x49\xfe\xa1\xdf\x83\x2d\x9d\xf6\x50\x68\x98\x1e\xba\xc4\x90\x3a\x0d\xf1\x0a\x27\x45\x87\xbd\xb6\xf5\x30\x5d\xd6\xf4\x50\xd4\xe3\x40\x38\x51\x49\xf5\xd1\xe9\x15\xae\xf3\xe0\xcb\x2b\x09\x70\xa9\x81\x48\xf9\xee\x73\x1f\x13\x2d\x68\x5c\x93\xd1\x06\x04\x67\x62\xfa\x1d\x4c\xa3\x1f\x31\x8c\x22\xe7\xcb\x82\x84\xe1\x09\x19\x39\xd0\xbf\x8a\x34\xe6\x6e\xa4\xaf\xb7\xf9\x6f\xb3\x01\x97\x9e\x90\x9b\xd0\xb2\xd4\x1e\x72\x70\x4e\x98\xbd\xb6\x5f\x57\xb1\x62\x0b\xfc\x52\xbd\x8f\xa5\x47\x41\xc8\x00\x14\x65\x86\x2b\x82\x6a\xfa\x4b\x3e\x2b\x82\x82\xdf\xb9\x58\x6d\x9d\x99\xd5\xfd\x87\x64\x61\xbc\xf3\x32\xa8\xa4\x08\x6c\x3d\x12\x6b\x49\x3b\xe3\xb6\x81\xe3\xbd\xae\x71\xb0\xe2\xda\x68\x1e\x1f\x15\xf4\x25\xf0\x8f\x05\x3f\x49\x49\x92\x89\x1b\x03\x79\xbe\xea\xfb\xe2\xe7\x16\xf1\x70\xd4\x22\x39\x8d\x9b\x9c\x58\x94\xe4\xfa\xad\x33\xa5\xf8\x86\x1d\xab\x59\xb4\xe2\x54\xd5\xee\xaf\xa1\x1a\x0b\xaa\x57\x7e\x8c\x24\x62\x7a\xc4\xb7\x36\x7d\xe2\x8e\x4b\x11\xd5\x64\xd7\x88\xb7\x14\x90\x59\xe4\x23\xec\xd4\x3f\x1a\xf6\xc2\x26\x4c\x16\x52\x38\x3e\xd4\xce\x0b\xbd\x9b\xe3\x61\xa2\x00\xf4\x99\xba\xde\x20\xd0\x3f\xa2\xa9\xfd\xc2\xad\x7e\xb3\x9b\x92\x95\x85\x07\x4b\xf8\x25\x26\x7b\x8a\x6a\xc6\x98\x20\x27\xba\x3c\x63\x02\xc5\xd2\x60\x68\x76\xb3\x1e\x80\x29\x25\xc0\x66\x25\xf9\xc4\xa2\xbb\x20\x0e\x20\x69\x05\x32\x08\x70\xc1\x80\xd3\xdd\xd1\x03\xec\xf3\xf6\x71\xda\xce\x12\xd4\x19\x57\xb2\x8b\xf9\x7e\xc3\x84\x9e\x5a\x35\x04\x6e\xdf\x7b\x67\x5e\x90\x9c\xe8\xea\xbb\xf0\x74\x1d\x33\x56\x81\x6b\x24\xfc\xb1\xe7\xba\xc8\x19\x03\xc6\x77\x40\xa1\xe8\x60\x4c\x6d\xe3\xf0\xe9\x48\xfd\x69\xb3\xf8\x6a\x0a\x8d\x96\x5e\x16\xa6\x68\xef\x6a\x11\x05\x45\x11\xe9\x77\x3b\x1e\xa7\xc4\x2a\xcc\xd9\xe6\x44\x59\xda\x9a\xae\x66\x91\x85\x02\xe3\x82\x7a\x24\x02\xbe\xb6\x91\x04\xa6\x29\xc8\x7d\xe3\x3b\x98\xd1\xd0\x2d\x1d\x4c\xea\x9b\xc1\x9e\x28\x27\x01\x66\x82\xff\xe3\x84\x29\xbd\xd8\x26\xd8\xa1\xa5\x07\x6c\x16\x59\x03\x04\x74\x25\xe5\x07\x1a\xff\x8b\x52\x88\xf9\x5c\x65\x98\xaf\x96\x62\x72\x17\x93\x77\xc8\x67\x37\x21\x2c\x67\xe6\x6f\x22\x9f\xd6\x10\x64\x9b\x6d\xcd\xaf\x41\xf9\x60\x3c\x9e\x14\xbc\xfd\x11\xd2\x03\xd2\xf1\x55\x6f\xcf\xdb\x93\xd7\xec\xda\x10\x30\xe0\x05\x46\xe5\x9e\xdc\x93\x78\xff\xb6\x4f\x4c\xc5\xab\x89\x30\x66\x3e\xf0\x15\x6a\x8b\xcd\x03\x2d\xad\x67\x3e\x35\xd3\x3c\x31\xc0\xda\xfd\xd2\x58\x3b\x8b\xa7\xa7\x79\xe6\xb3\xc5\xa2\x0d\x4e\x28\xc5\x5b\x8b\x03\xef\x6c\x83\xb9\xe7\x7f\x88\x40\x08\xca\x09\xc8\x9f\x98\xf3\xdc\x89\xf4\x88\xe8\x7f\x28\xde\x5b\x1d\xcd\xa5\x7d\x3c\x44\xa6\x0e\xca\xdd\x34\xf6\xfa\x58\x8b\x41\xac\x47\x34\xe3\xdc\x35\x24\x68\x48\x06\x89\xa4\xa7\x69\x37\x8d\x1d\x89\x75\xfa\xc0\xfe\xc5\x73\x6c\x01\xee\xa3\x0c\x4a\x09\xed\x9f\x29\x6e\xb9\xbe\xf4\x89\x97\x5a\xa9\x19\x27\x56\x9e\xea\x00\x56\x1c\xe5\x94\x32\x46\x72\xa7\xa9\x20\xf0\x4e\x4a\x80\xac\x0c\xe2\x8e\x3b\x89\x28\x1b\x83\xb9\xbf\x67\x46\x4d\x2e\xc2\x8e\x20\xb2\x04\xb2\x53\xa8\x0b\xee\xd5\xad\x66\x04\x16\x55\x81\x19\x1e\xe0\xf5\x5b\xb5\x3a\xf5\x73\x3b\x1d\x4b\x85\xb2\xc8\x72\x88\x2d\xd4\xcf\xbb\xa6\x78\xb0\xc7\xf1\x7c\x62\x31\x8b\x43\x8e\x0a\xba\x97\x5e\x04\x4d\x8c\xbe\x22\xa6\x96\x29\x3f\xdb\x79\xb4\x85\x6e\xa6\x05\x65\xc8\x0e\xea\xdd\x9a\xc9\xd6\x9b\xaf\x9e\x7e\xc5\x88\x56\x73\xeb\x08\xec\x88\x47\x07\x61\xb6\x5a\xf3\x77\xba\xd6\x30\xdb\x9b\x9b\xe7\x2a\xea\xea\xbb\x72\x3d\x65\x34\x5b\x07\xf7\xc4\x71\x98\x65\x6a\x8e\x21\xcb\x5b\xaa\xbe\x34\xe9\x25\xd7\xbb\x9d\x5c\x6b\xac\x46\xed\x27\xa4\x23\x97\x4f\x ea\xf8\xad\x1f\xed\x03\x94\x74\xbd\x95\xfd\x2e\x67\xc1\xd7\x6f\x11\xd2\x99\xa7\xfd\xe4\xb5\xef\x13\x61\x2e\xa6\x75\x07\xd1\xc5\x0c\xb2\xb8\x6f\x50\x77\xc6\x95\x0a\x11\x9d\xc4\xab\xca\x8b\x08\x87\xe4\xf2\xa8\xc5\x76\x20\xeb\xe1\x71\xd1\x46\x5a\x3e\x4a\x76\x2d\x71\x0d\x98\xcb\x30\x55\x0d\x3d\x88\x18\x23\x55\x8f\x53\x3b\xae\xc7\x81\x3f\x17\xab\x5b\xf2\x1e\x5d\x96\xda\xcb\x01\x53\xa1\xba\x88\x47\xf4\xec\x9b\x3e\x75\x10\x44\xb9\xb2\xe4\x7f\xaf\x28\xf5\x44\xf9\x17\xd7\x13\x3c\x82\x26\xf9\x97\x2e\xa8\x55\x49\x91\x28\x94\xd9\x55\x52\x82\x51\x86\x23\x49\xdb\x2b\x3b\x68\x7e\x17\x08\x5e\x1a\x28\xe2\xcf\xb3\x2e\xe2\x75\x5c\x4c\x8b\x84\xda\x6b\x25\x9a\x30\x22\x2d\x9a\x58\x9f\x7b\xb5\xef\x40\x09\x83\x96\xa0\xdc\x7b\x99\x93\xd8\x88\x3a\xc8\xbe\x2f\xf2\x32\xe0\x23\x06\xf3\xd5\x80\xac\x38\x96\xee\xb7\xad\x85\x11\xf9\xd7\xe4\x0f\x12\x7b\xa4\x41\x02\x06\x84\xb0\xb7\x2f\x38\x35\xae\xef\xc8\xa0\x5a\x3c\x7d\x0d\x58\x73\xa7\xa7\xc2\x53\x95\x77\x74\xfe\x36\xe4\x70\x50\xec\x39\xfe\xfb\xfa\xb9\x2a\x2a\x8c\x01\x08\x0e\x40\x27\xad\xf1\xfc\xce\xb4\xc0\x97\x53\xdb\x97\x88\xca\x3c\x9e\xb1\x4a\xd2\xd7\xf9\x24\xda\x58\x1b\x48\x77\x22\xa6\x1c\x45\xb1\x40\x04\x22\x1a\x26\x91\xaf\xc7\xba\xcc\xe3\x6a\xd5\xf6\xf4\x11\xf9\x8e\x9a\xa6\x52\xdd\x54\xfd\x06\x9f\x69\xdc\xad\xfb\x25\x90\x14\x28\xb0\x62\xc7\xac\x5a\xf2\x8f\xa9\x80\x2e\xcf\xcc\x64\x08\xa5\xe4\x16\xc7\xe0\xe8\xe7\x28\xae\x7a\x02\x58\x9f\xf5\x79\x17\xfc\xad\x83\xc8\x18\xa5\x9c\x01\x00\x8b\x35\xd6\x37\x19\xee\x91\x3a\xc2\x66\xf6\xd1\x04\xbc\x38\x1a\xd0\x02\xc6\xd5\xf8\xfc\xa5\xaa\xc3\xcd\x95\x25\xeb\x0e\xb2\x93\xd7\x9e\xb8\xcf\x41\xa9\xe7\x4f\x43\x04\xb9\x55\x61\x57\xeb\x60\x9c\x1a\x7b\x38\x87\xe8\x62\xb4\x4b\x7a\x0c\x8d\x54\xfc\xe4\x7c\x35\xfd\x21\xe8\x72\xd7\xbe\x5f\x20\x61\x65\xdb\x5c\xb1\x1d\x3b\xcd\xcc\x2b\x0c\xd8\xbd\x16\x95\x66\xf8\xe6\x0d\xba\x24\xac\xc1\x24\xad\x1d\x59\x71\xb9\x87\x2e\x8e\x92\x57\x80\xf7\x33\xc6\xb6\x8b\xd5\x2b\xb9\xa5\x71\x40\x83\xc7\xbd\xca\xf2\x59\x1e\xf4\xbf\x9f\x24\x95\xc6\x52\xb3\x52\x09\xb1\x4a\x8b\xf8\x30\xfe\x6d\x b6\xf0\x6f\x73\x4e\x71\xa2\x96\xd0\xc4\x3e\xb5\x94\xb0\x67\xd5\x7b\xb8\x4f\x4a\x2d\xa5\xa3\x2c\x9d\x7f\x01\x6d\xdc\x04\xed\x40\x4e\xbd\xf1\x6f\x9f\xa7\x51\xbd\x09\x40\xb9\xb3\xa1\x4e\x7d\x30\xa0\x94\xab\xeb\x6b\x3f\x48\x1e\x85\xab\xe4\xdf\x22\xf5\xc1\x14\xc1\xdc\x2b\xd7\xe4\x66\xd2\xfe\x21\x00\x8d\x45\xda\x0c\xa8\x53\xae\x43\xb0\x27\x06\x95\x52\x83\x78\xf4\xc6\x1c\x22\x89\xcd\x78\xa2\x44\xee\x86\x56\x17\x07\xd0\x0b\xc3\xee\x6a\x6c\x93\xe0\x05\xa3\x69\x80\x25\x24\xc7\x4e\xa0\x3e\x45\x98\xde\x8b\xb0\x92\x4c\x91\xf8\x96\x19\x8b\xc1\xed\xa4\x74\x56\xdd\xb7\xb2\x04\xd8\x5c\xcb\x16\xe9\xb9\x0b\x47\x52\xf8\xf8\xa6\x58\x43\x57\x48\x8e\x72\x53\x13\x23\x56\x9c\x88\x31\x61\x34\x37\x1f\xcc\x00\xa3\xad\x42\x0f\x8c\x00\x73\xb9\x90\xad\x8e\x71\xb7\xc3\xef\x06\xa9\xec\xce\xf2\x10\xa9\xa0\x5e\x9f\xc5\x72\xf7\xf4\xdf\xf9\x28\x76\x21\x49\x6b\xff\xdb\x68\xec\xf2\x8e\xac\x29\x74\x14\x8e\xd0\x5e\xc4\x34\x93\x4f\x53\x0f\xb4\x3b\xfe\x38\xa8\xe2\x07\xd4\x92\xb7\xf7\xba\x90\x81\x92\x3f\xdb\x0e\x55\x1d\xa0\xbb\x85\xb1\x39\xe3\x67\xf1\xef\x5e\x04\x3d\x5e\x0a\x7f\x5c\x14\xa1\x41\x96\x05\x06\xfe\x6a\xb8\x8f\xb1\xdf\x6f\xf7\x21\xe2\xae\x64\x63\x70\xbe\x3f\xf5\xbc\xc4\xd0\x96\x91\x0b\xc5\x7c\xdc\xcc\xcb\x28\x34\x02\xb7\x8a\xc5\x18\xba\x3f\xe9\x31\xd1\x24\xb3\x08\x60\x90\x5b\xc1\x4c\xe3\xda\x8a\xea\x53\x95\x22\xa2\x60\x7c\x73\xae\xb9\x18\xa1\xda\xd5\x84\x92\x90\xbf\x8d\x35\xfe\xfe\xcd\x3c\xd0\x83\x19\x72\x39\xa0\x6d\x82\xe8\x2f\x33\xa2\xc3\x68\x44\xc2\x37\xa4\x2b\x31\x61\x0c\xe2\xf7\xab\xaf\x5f\x90\x16\xff\x04\x86\x57\x61\x1d\xb4\x2d\xf3\xca\x3c\x58\xd9\x2a\x90\xd3\x08\xed\x81\x99\xee\xf9\x74\x75\x66\xf2\xf8\x3a\xca\x37\x83\x00\x2c\xbd\x27\xf7\x37\x09\x18\x7a\xa3\xa5\xdb\x72\xee\xd4\xad\x6a\x4c\xf8\x74\x52\x9a\x00\x10\xb5\x31\xa7\x24\xc1\x36\x4f\xbf\x4e\xfd\x78\x31\x72\x01\x7e\xa3\x60\x58\xf5\x63\xc5\x40\xce\x7f\xd5\x90\x78\xc3\xda\x92\xca\xab\xbc\xf5\x61\x9a\x12\x93\x09\x19\xa8\x05\x7b\x8e\x2c\xad\x3f\xa4\xde\x6b\x39\x20\x2a\x5f\x72\x8b\xba\xf5\x26\xd0\x72\xcc\x38\x50\x68\xcd\x65\xa7\xa2\x08\x4e\x0c\x9a\x04\x35\xa0\x1c\x38\x2f\x9a\xd4\xa2\x00\x1d\x06\x38\xe0\x62\xdd\x44\xf3\xe5\xc4\x6e\x56\x34\xda\x88\xf9\xd5\x27\xf0\x50\x2d\x46\x3b\x89\xa5\x5c\xaf\x89\xd2\xe4\xf2\xbf\x3f\xd7\xd1\x9b\x90\xd4\x32\x58\x60\xef\xba\x48\xa9\xdf\x6e\x09\x69\xa2\xc8\xe4\xd2\xe0\x14\x1d\x32\x59\x4b\xf3\x72\xaa\xe9\xcc\x45\xa6\xf7\xa9\x46\x5d\x8d\x9f\xd4\xc7\x2f\x5a\x46\x98\xc9\x7b\xb8\x99\xcb\x4d\x46\xb4\x55\x26\x6f\x17\x4d\xa3\xf9\xd0\xc6\xc6\xde\xfc\x74\xdd\x23\x5f\xe2\x46\xe5\x78\xf0\xe2\x7a\x80\x21\x33\x37\x17\x65\x81\x81\x55\x80\x73\x5b\xf0\x00\xc0\x14\x1d\xef\xc4\xbe\x34\x55\x00\xe5\x02\xe1\x29\x05\x94\x7d\x93\x8f\x7b\x88\x40\x72\xec\xe5\xcd\x33\xf5\x93\x88\xb9\x85\xdc\xcc\x2c\x87\x5c\x85\xdd\x43\xcc\x8c\xbe\x1e\xa4\x81\xec\xbb\xe3\x6d\x5a\xdd\x72\xd0\x1e\xfb\x4c\x24\xe5\xf7\x30\x0a\x43\x4f\xcb\x10\x27\xbb\xb6\x8e\x4e\xb1\x00\x43\xb6\x10\x3c\xfa\xf0\x2b\xdf\x52\x6a\x80\x9f\x7a\xdb\x5c\x99\xbb\x00\xcb\x66\xdf\x2f\x1b\xc9\x82\x8b\x95\x58\xfb\x4d\x4c\x87\xb0\x8e\xd7\x54\x24\x44\x7d\xb1\x6a\x0c\x85\xf1\x4f\xbb\x67\xb8\x24\xcc\x45\x99\x72\x5a\x50\xea\x34\x89\x36\x48\x5e\x09\xce\x98\xdf\x5e\x09\xa6\x41\x32\x4c\xd4\x24\xd6\xd9\xb0\xbd\xd7\x4a\x4c\x3f\xd4\x6c\xdb\xaf\xb2\x56\xcb\x57\x00\xef\x59\xe0\x9a\x1c\x84\x9f\x84\xc6\xbf\xb8\xd4\x1e\x45\x1a\xec\x75\x6b\x06\x5c\xd7\xad\xb1\x00\x4c\x74\xdd\x4e\x6d\x95\x20\xfa\xfd\x23\x8e\xde\x0c\xb7\x6a\x40\x95\xe1\x11\x36\xc1\xd3\x76\x77\xd2\x71\x0b\x6a\xe2\x97\xe6\xeb\x14\xb6\xc6\x33\xec\xe3\x5a\xca\x91\xf6\xc1\xdb\xad\x2c\x20\xa0\x9a\x0b\x61\x9d\x64\x6e\xb1\x79\xc9\xd8\xcf\x1d\x9f\xd1\x73\x80\x12\x9d\x88\xe4\x92\x5f\xca\xdd\x8d\xf6\xb7\x1f\x6e\x11\xd9\x23\x90\x1b\x9f\x4d\x45\x2b\xf0\x7f\xb9\x2f\xe9\x65\x5a\xec\xd8\x57\x68\xd9\xa2\x6f\xa1\x82\x27\x17\x55\xdb\xf8\x20\x89\xda\xa2\xad\x14\x5e\x89\x77\xde\x70\x4b\x26\xaa\xd8\x58\x08\x3b\xc5\x03\x50\xc6\xa8\xde\x14\x70\xdb\x1e\xf8\x16\xdc\x2b\xc1\x7a\x73\xa6\xad\xc7\x49\x82\x34\x65\xaa\x25\xbb\xd0\xab\xa9\x05\x88\x81\x35\x10\x12\x32\xd4\x91\x48\x2d\x06\x55\x03\x04\x69\x4e\xd5\x2d\xf1\xcf\x92\x24\x15\x1d\xd8\xf2\xa2\xc5\xaa\xd5\xf1\x12\x47\x58\xf1\x4d\x94\xdf\xfd\x38\x0c\x59\xc3\x9e\x82\x7d\xd4\x32\x0a\x34\xf7\x8d\x3e\xd6\xfe\x0c\x13\xb3\xcf\xea\xe8\x17\xac\xc7\x9b\xf1\xba\xef\xf8\x0c\x6f\x24\xfc\x90\xe8\x15\x67\x46\x3e\xfb\x88\x89\xbf\xc5\x5a\x2f\x73\x91\xaf\xde\x08\x07\xf4\x84\x7d\x60\x99\x90\xe4\xf4\x67\xe3\xa7\xa4\x5f\x8e\xf3\x9f\x89\x9d\x13\x23\x20\xc4\x39\x5d\x8d\xcb\xc5\x2c\x74\x6d\x27\x1a\x6f\xf5\x0c\x72\xad\xaa\x7f\x30\x64\x85\x92\xbf\x4d\x80\xf0\x32\x6c\x88\xb6\xc9\x5f\x88\x37\xb5\xb9\xef\x59\x74\x02\x89\x58\x4a\x74\x81\x6c\xc9\xc9\x2e\xbc\xbf\x06\xa5\xc7\x61\xac\x78\x74\xd6\xf2\x5a\xa0\xe7\xd8\xe1\xe8\xc1\x93\x8c\x57\x03\x94\x82\x55\x0a\x5f\xc1\xda\x3b\x4c\x66\x9e\x87\x0a\x6a\xa4\x97\x90\xd1\xdc\x06\xcc\x50\x95\x76\x2a\x62\xb3\x2a\xd2\xf6\xc2\xa3\x42\xa5\x8e\x89\xe7\x15\xbd\x99\x6e\x61\x69\xf3\x83\xbf\x95\xbf\x8b\x19\x14\xb0\xf7\xa4\x14\x88\x8b\x5b\x27\xd0\xce\x1f\x90\xc4\xf9\xa6\x58\xea\x12\x78\xe0\x96\x0b\xa0\x14\x2f\x57\x9d\xf0\x29\x4c\x27\x21\x4c\x2e\x79\xa4\x09\x5e\x4c\xfe\x7a\xed\x9f\x87\x6e\x73\xe3\x0e\xcb\x25\xbe\x55\x74\xf7\x8a\x75\xcf\x7a\xe2\xff\xc7\xbe\x68\x5e\x18\x08\xcd\xd7\xee\x48\xf9\x10\xdf\x1d\x10\xb2\x90\x9f\xc6\x49\x38\x88\x40\xc3\xe2\xca\x42\xc6\x92\x79\xfe\xe0\xc6\x54\xec\x9c\xc8\x5b\x25\x91\x42\xf8\xda\x76\x90\x6c\xd0\x01\x7f\x9a\x1c\x2e\xcf\x4f\x21\xe6\x50\x20\x9c\xb1\xb4\x07\x83\x01\xce\x9a\x43\x8e\x3a\x9d\x8e\x29\xf0\x5b\x29\xdf\xf1\x3a\x71\xb7\x0b\x64\x65\x70\x49\x93\x9e\xba\xc6\x48\x78\x84\xda\x7e\x80\x5c\x58\xae\xbb\xf4\x82\xcf\xcd\x43\xe7\xdf\xca\xef\xc4\xe5\xbc\x2f\xab\xb6\x7a\xb8\x26\x14\x91\x92\x2d\xae\x08\xf0\x3d\x44\xb1\xa2\x72\xb8\x6f\xbf\xe6\x84\x2c\xbe\x39\x3f\x44\xcf\xbf\x7e\x6c\x42\x71\x23\x4e\x28\x5b\xca\xca\x9e\xb9\xcd\x35\x57\x32\xc3\x3d\x39\x1d\x0b\xdc\xe4\xd1\xcc\x9d\x9f\x6c\x7b\x3d\x3d\x34\x06\x35\xa2\xb5\xe7\xf3\xad\x28\xe9\x64\xae\x43\xd7\xd8\x1e\x03\x87\xeb\x27\x7c\xe5\xd9\xaa\xfa\x7d\xf4\x68\xe7\xf7\x5a\xfe\x52\xb0\x40\xfc\x01\x13\x0b\x5a\x57\x46\xe2\xdc\x00\x3c\xbd\x1c\xa3\x42\x11\xd9\x83\x1a\x19\x66\xf1\x6f\xd4\x17\x49\x67\x9d\xfa\x26\x9f\x76\x2a\x21\x1e\x8d\x2f\x8d\x92\xa3\xbf\x30\x87\x44\xb3\xa8\xff\x27\x0b\x2f\x67\xdc\x55\x4c\x52\xb8\x04\x02\xa9\xff\x4f\xbe\xc3\x8c\xe0\x2d\x9a\x1f\x93\x0b\x1d\x2a\x4b\xd9\x8a\x6a\x67\xce\xc5\x39\x4c\x6c\xe9\x71\x36\x91\x5d\xcf\x94\xca\x26\x0f\x1b\x56\xf9\x82\xf1\xf4\x51\xfe\x8a\xff\x78\x30\x41\xd8\x6b\x65\x94\x59\xe6\xdf\x6a\x80\xb0\xf3\x49\xd5\x50\x6b\x10\x25\x5f\xa7\xcc\xf3\xec\xd9\x0c\x82\xb2\x92\x4a\x55\x31\x87\x69\xf4\x5a\x26\x1d\x4c\x67\xf8\x75\x3f\x66\xd6\xef\x9f\x8c\xec\xad\x6e\x8f\xe2\xf9\x25\x90\x5d\x20\x56\xe2\x9a\x99\x49\x75\x03\x40\x7b\x76\x3b\xbc\x87\x32\xab\x02\x97\xc3\x45\xbe\xa7\xc7\x03\xb5\xde\xa0\x75\x14\xfd\x9c\xd4\x19\x98\x01\x05\x29\xc0\x76\x83\x78\xb9\xc5\x1e\xf3\x70\xf8\x5c\x4e\xad\xb2\xd6\xe6\x11\xf8\x0d\xf8\xea\xab\x64\x23\x53\xbb\xad\xf6\xff\xe1\x54\xce\x84\x9f\x65\x79\x9d\x7a\x82\x16\xb0\x50\x40\xfb\xc9\x4c\x8d\xbc\xfc\x25\x25\x27\x5e\x4d\x8a\xa8\x21\x66\x61\xc7\xc9\x61\x89\x9b\x61\x3d\x8a\xa9\xe4\xaf\x84\x8b\x31\x72\x7e\xad\x6f\x21\x42\x8a\x71\x52\x82\xe9\x10\x72\x12\x26\xb9\xf5\xf1\xa7\x19\xcb\xb0\x4e\x56\x1d\x69\x87\x8b\x90\xc4\x37\x09\x0a\x16\xce\x6e\xe6\xf9\x4b\x90\xba\xf9\xc1\xf4\xfa\x49\x9a\x88\xfc\xd2\x78\x63\x13\x93\x6e\x38\x6a\x62\x6b\x5e\xff\xae\x65\xd2\xf5\xe4\x1b\xb6\x71\x2d\x46\x27\xc6\x37\x8d\x72\x38\x39\x83\x7d\xdb\x40\x07\x70\x45\x9e\xa0\x30\xc0\x76\xaf\x74\xfd\xdb\xf7\x60\x38\xbf\x4c\x20\xdf\x57\xe5\x15\x3b\x7a\x5e\xc5\x41\x4c\xf0\xd7\x3c\x61\xd3\x22\x64\x99\x28\x82\x6a\x3d\x7b\x84\xb1\x23\xde\x12\xfc\x5b\x8b\x5c\x04\xc2\x76\x99\x96\x24\xc3\xa8\xa4\x11\xd7\xcb\x8a\xee\xdd\xfd\x24\x94\xa0\x17\x47\x41\x8f\x4d\x87\x7d\x30\x3e\x50\x04\xef\x1a\x01\xbc\x0a\x70\x12\x2d\x02\x79\x75\xf1\x84\xc3\x5a\x4c\xde\x2b\x83\xa9\xe6\x1c\xca\xe3\x6c\x98\xb9\x2d\x08\x34\x65\xfa\x1b\xd3\x29\x45\x58\x67\xa7\x2a\xfe\x5c\x0d\x84\x14\xc3\x6a\x02\x8a\x51\xa7\x57\x7a\x06\x91\xb7\xa5\xa7\xd6\x2f\xd5\x08\x59\xc8\xcc\x23\xda\x89\xd9\x6d\x38\x6d\xb7\x7b\x26\x3f\x5c\xb8\x2c\x11\x17\xa8\xcd\x35\x26\x70\x2e\x17\x3c\xac\x8e\x53\xaa\x33\xfa\x20\xe3\x95\xe5\x40\xa1\xe9\x0e\x65\xa0\xcb\x69\xec\xc3\x9f\x55\x79\x6e\xa6\x77\xaf\x74\x7a\x60\x17\x26\x69\x2c\xf0\xcc\xbf\x72\xcb\x93\xf4\x24\x22\xaf\xdd\x41\xc1\xfb\x62\xa7\x9d\xb6\xf6\x75\xb4\x08\x1f\x89\x77\xfa\xdc\x8b\xbd\x9d\x53\x48\xbb\x64\x46\x27\x36\xac\xcd\x97\x78\x5d\x4e\xd1\xe0\xfb\x9c\x7f\x7c\xc6\x4d\x62\xc5\x1a\xd9\xe4\x27\xc8\xb1\x01\xd4\xa9\xf8\x4c\xfe\xd7\xa7\xed\x2f\x72\x76\xf6\x6e\xd2\xf2\xf7\xcb\x5e\xf9\x72\x79\xc0\x86\xe5\x1b\x10\x7e\xda\x16\x17\x7d\x14\xae\xec\x9b\x32\x16\x9b\x46\x5a\x7a\x5c\x08\x24\x40\x49\xd0\xe1\x91\x38\x22\xf0\x89\xde\x90\x1a\xb8\x1c\x5a\x82\xc5\xcd\x3a\xdc\x19\xb8\x94\xa1\x2b\x78\xb4\x8e\xe9\xfc\x96\xd6\xae\xb0\x94\x0a\xd9\x95\x48\x76\x2e\x3c\xce\x58\x75\x70\xfa\xe0\x4e\x96\xcb\xca\x02\xc4\xbf\xb5\xab\xbd\x0f\xf7\xb4\xfe\x53\x56\xd1\xcc\xce\x1d\x74\x84\x95\x4f\xbd\xd7\x7d\x54\x6c\x7a\xfc\x4b\x7c\x47\x41\x4f\x4d\xbb\x94\x84\x02\x6e\x76\x8e\xf0\x86\x24\xe3\x59\xb5\x34\x81\x68\x67\xfa\x2d\xf5\x55\xae\x64\xda\x03\xb8\xea\x05\x8e\x2f\x61\x7e\x09\x75\xd9\x3a\x6f\x4d\xe8\x63\x6e\x82\xdb\x18\x75\x9d\x52\x41\x18\x82\x8c\x15\x75\x6a\xde\x59\xbd\xed\x53\xa8\x70\x46\x2e\x20\x17\x6b\xf0\x22\xc8\x13\x74\x74\xb0\x92\xbd\x0f\x80\x0f\x30\x3c\xa4\x0d\x1a\xed\x29\x0f\xc9\xc4\x22\x98\x54\xea\x0e\x28\xe5\x30\x93\x99\x35\xa0\x61\x57\x47\x4b\x98\x3d\xfe\xce\xd9\x49\xaa\x12\x6f\xf9\xb0\x47\x30\x18\xed\xec\xd1\x42\xe6\x8c\x55\x66\x1d\xc7\x76\xdb\x48\xa0\x8d\x14\x2b\xe0\x94\x7b\xbd\x9b\x1d\x96\x4a\xac\x66\xcc\x87\x6e\x89\x31\xc0\xce\x49\xc8\x67\x70\x9d\x1f\x89\x5f\xe4\x57\x54\x9f\x12\xa4\x8c\xb6\xa5\xe3\x88\xf9\x14\x14\xf0\xa9\x12\x4e\x2c\x25\x88\xee\x4a\x93\xff\xa6\xd4\xad\x67\x50\x87\xd0\xd0\x18\xbb\x04\x16\xdd\xd3\x58\xbc\xf7\x67\xfd\xa3\xdb\xa8\x06\xf8\x1f\xfd\xc9\x6d\x64\xb4\x04\xb6\x2c\xad\x21\xa8\xc7\xe1\x2a\x27\x5d\x58\xc9\x38\x0d\x6e\xac\xea\x4d\x64\xe8\x55\x64\xf7\xfb\xff\x02\x5a\x55\x52\xd0\xf9\x7b\xd9\x89\x0c\x25\xb1\x5f\x18\x23\x03\xd1\x2d\x26\xf7\x11\x98\xfa\x50\x96\xb7\x62\x27\x39\x41\xc2\x4e\xec\x61\xcd\xfd\x74\x50\xe2\x9a\x16\x39\xd8\x83\x31\x8d\x44\x77\xda\xe9\xba\x34\xcb\xc4\xc3\xf8\x05\xf4\xb4\x90\xc2\xd9\x69\x58\x66\xf6\xc8\x71\xc6\xb4\x49\xf3\xdd\x33\xa2\x75\xd7\xe0\xc5\xe4\x33\x1b\xab\xac\x51\x41\x06\x3d\x09\xf3\xae\x24\xd3\x5b\x0a\x66\x8e\x67\x87\xf1\x6e\x04\xe6\x43\xe6\x2e\x0f\xab\x22\xf8\xbb\xbe\x5c\x4a\x40\xf5\x30\x3f\x51\x79\x85\x30\x6c\x35\x86\xc2\xc5\xa1\x5b\x07\x61\x79\x2c\x23\xeb\x04\xe4\x78\x66\x11\x94\xaa\x5b\xd9\x67\xfb\x78\xe1\xe9\xa0\x55\x9c\x72\xfe\xa6\x1c\xfd\x9b\xac\xa7\xbf\x8d\xe6\x2d\x51\xab\x02\xc9\x5c\xa7\x19\x96\xb2\x53\xbe\x4b\xf6\x0e\xad\x62\xf8\x21\xc0\x03\x19\x49\x2a\x0f\x8c\x29\x3f\x3d\xdf\xa4\x73\xb1\x06\xc2\xde\x04\xf3\xfa\x37\x62\x61\x84\x70\x9d\xdb\x95\x7a\xc5\x23\x52\xe6\xc6\x1a\xc4\x82\x5b\x26\x5f\xe8\x1e\x71\x82\x8a\x9e\x5f\x0e\x0f\xef\x16\xb5\xe2\xb1\x58\xaf\x40\x1f\xd5\xb5\xfc\x1f\x46\x38\x10\xa4\x5c\x02\x09\x68\xa0\x0e\xd9\x17\xed\x75\xc1\x8d\xd4\x3e\xb4\x10\xcb\x0f\x27\xeb\xca\xc8\xd3\x6b\xb1\xf6\x57\x6e\xd4\x6b\x30\x93\x04\x9b\x72\x8b\x20\x63\xc2\xaf\x48\xfa\x35\x9c\xc8\x2c\xf4\x21\xc8\xf1\xea\x17\xa3\xe2\x1c\x55\xb8\xed\xe9\x50\x5b\x1c\x27\x97\x97\x98\x27\x94\xd6\x7d\xad\x88\xf0\x4c\xea\x13\x5f\x7e\xda\x8f\x7e\x3c\x8a\xfd\x0d\xe8\x27\x3c\x96\x59\xe4\x3d\x5b\x2f\xe2\xc4\x6b\x1c\xf3\x8f\x9e\xb8\xe4\xcb\xd1\xa3\xec\x69\x79\x68\x33\x08\xae\xa8\x79\x9b\x87\x29\x91\xbe\x31\xd9\x4e\xbd\x93\x1e\x27\x56\x24\xe8\xa0\x30\x8b\xa2\xfe\xa0\xce\xb4\x2b\xc5\xdf\x60\x59\xc0\xc2\xec\x52\x64\x65\x6c\x66\xf9\x96\x46\x1a\x59\xd1\x97\x31\x2a\xa4\xc3\x75\x83\xd0\x42\x40\xe7\xf4\x20\x28\x2c\xbc\xf6\x87\x48\xa0\xf4\xa7\x59\x0e\x14\xca\xd2\x0a\xad\xe5\xba\x18\xff\x29\x69\x00\xe5\x56\x8f\xbe\xf4\xb8\x4e\x25\xc2\x00\x70\x82\x73\x20\xc9\xda\x37\xa2\x87\xc5\x17\x0e\xdc\x7f\x45\x29\xe1\x0f\x5d\x75\xd3\x37\xbd\xf9\xc5\x13\x7b\xfd\x6f\x66\x5c\x61\x83\xb5\xb9\x6a\x51\x87\xda\xcb\x1f\xc5\x30\xa8\xf9\x66\x49\xda\xfc\x4c\x03\x03\x33\x91\x14\xf0\x5a\x24\xa7\x2d\x61\x1c\x89\x93\x55\xfa\x36\x10\x03\x47\x8a\x48\x05\xa3\xa6\x45\x68\x3e\xd5\xe1\x7d\xa5\x9e\xdc\xd6\xfb\x77\xea\x10\xf5\x0c\x47\xcf\xd1\x9f\x2f\x8d\x10\x93\xe0\xe0\x44\x07\x14\xb5\x29\xeb\xc4\xe2\x78\xd9\x67\x4b\x84\xee\xc5\xd2\x90\xe0\x20\x8f\xb5\xd8\x0a\x3f\xe3\x11\x21\x99\x9c\x66\xea\x08\x3c\xa0\x9c\xb3\x0a\x78\xf1\x7a\x01\x92\xbd\x15\x7e\x92\x16\x67\x3d\x3c\x39\xe8\x15\x7b\x89\xfa\xe9\x9e\x7d\xa4\x04\x75\xc1\xe4\xd0\xf9\x4c\x1b\x9c\xf2\xbd\x9d\x1d\xb8\xdc\xc4\x29\x3d\x19\x96\xa9\x47\x2c\x98\xa1\xc5\xc9\x14\x6f\x07\x18\x95\x61\x30\x05\x18\xf7\x8b\xa9\x40\x7b\xf4\xd0\x36\xf0\x8a\xbd\x20\xb5\x18\x02\x71\xaf\xd9\xdb\xbf\xc7\x81\x66\x7a\xf8\xcc\x5e\xa5\x0a\xb7\x20\x85\x58\x5b\x02\x8a\x06\x53\x40\xe1\x0b\xe8\x12\x24\xd0\xb3\x1b\x0f\xcd\x92\xb0\x06\xa9\x36\x63\x91\x27\x63\x82\x79\x86\x2b\x31\xe2\xf3\x16\xcd\xed\x92\x40\x68\xd6\x7d\x94\x2f\xc4\x61\xa0\xdc\xca\xfe\x84\xd5\xba\x6d\x02\xa1\x63\x60\xd1\x5d\xf1\xd0\xfd\x3f\x21\xd9\x6d\x22\x82\x3a\xdd\xc9\x64\xac\xd9\x04\x25\xaf\x55\xae\xff\x70\x18\x25\x7a\x17\xa0\x04\x15\xbd\x75\x7e\xfd\xfc\xdf\xc3\x09\xb8\xfe\x53\xd2\xba\xdb\xf4\x45\xfe\xcd\xd8\x86\xd4\x2a\x50\xb1\xbc\x93\x2a\x0f\x8b\x52\x98\xcd\xc3\x41\x2f\xa7\x30\xf5\xaf\xd8\xc7\x32\x4b\x02\x02\xe3\x71\x9a\x30\x1d\xf6\x81\x35\x57\x0b\x8e\x1b\x69\x47\x91\xec\x6f\x36\x06\xd3\xd8\x96\x43\x9b\x34\xae\x3e\x10\x1f\x73\xfc\xf8\x53\x74\x80\x57\xd7\xef\x92\x63\x83\xda\x7e\x8c\x6b\x93\x79\x00\x50\x06\xa1\x64\xec\xb7\x0a\xcf\x35\x0c\xee\x80\xf3\x82\x67\x86\xa3\x64\xc8\xc5\x7a\x86\xae\x2c\x03\xaa\x11\x27\x17\x3d\xec\xcb\x96\x11\x8b\xf1\xc3\x0c\x40\xee\xa0\xec\xd4\xfa\x5a\xc0\x1a\xf5\xb5\x53\x38\x55\x8e\xc4\x46\xbe\x90\xe5\x68\x7b\xcd\x33\x90\xc0\x25\x69\x3d\x97\x9c\xe1\x1d\xe0\x60\x17\x25\xd0\xc9\x28\x89\x33\x11\x2b\x4a\x53\xf7\x2d\x6d\x5c\xee\x2d\xbb\xae\x8a\x7d\x61\xef\x09\x6c\xea\x24\xb4\xe3\xa2\xbd\xab\xe0\xf6\x10\xc4\xda\xab\x6d\xe3\x0f\x9e\x7b\x49\x9a\xa6\x66\x42\x68\x53\xb5\x44\xe8\x4c\x17\xa4\x27\x91\xf2\x02\x6a\xcd\xa7\x1e\x68\x6c\x14\x14\xa0\x81\xe8\x27\xa6\xc5\x66\xfe\xdd\xeb\x0b\x70\xeb\x53\x08\xa7\xe6\x56\x75\xf5\x22\x0c\xbd\xec\x09\xdb\x8d\xa1\x3b\xde\x75\xf2\x5a\x29\x +_B='diag'
+_A=None
+import numpy as _np
+from dataclasses import dataclass as _dataclass
+from typing import List
+import itertools
+@_dataclass
+class SingleBin:
+	means:0;weights:0;covariances:0;area:0;name:0
+	@property
+	def as_gmm(self):A=self;from sklearn.mixture import GaussianMixture as C;B=C(n_components=len(A.weights),covariance_type=_B);B.fit(A.means);B.means_=A.means;B.weights_=A.weights;B.covariances_=A.covariances;return B
+	def sample(A,n):return A.as_gmm.sample(n)[0]
+	def plot(A,dims=_A,**C):
+		B=dims;import plotly.express as D
+		if B:return D.scatter(x=A.means[:,B[0]],y=A.means[:,B[1]],error_x=_np.sqrt(A.covariances[:,B[0]]),error_y=_np.sqrt(A.covariances[:,B[1]]),size=A.weights,**C)
+		if A.means.shape[1]>1:return D.scatter(x=A.means[:,0],y=A.means[:,1],error_x=_np.sqrt(A.covariances[:,0]),error_y=_np.sqrt(A.covariances[:,1]),size=A.weights,**C)
+		return D.scatter(x=A.means[:,0],error_x=_np.sqrt(A.covariances[:,0]),size=A.weights,**C)
+class BinningScheme:
+	def __init__(A):A.bins=[]
+	def append(A,input):A.bins.append(input)
+	def extend(A,input):A.bins.extend(input)
+	@property
+	def means(self):return _np.stack([A.means for A in self.bins])
+	@property
+	def weights(self):return _np.stack([A.weights*A.area for A in self.bins])
+	@property
+	def covariances(self):return _np.stack([A.covariances for A in self.bins])
+	def to_dict(A,batch_tiles=1):B=batch_tiles;return{'bin_means':[A.means.tolist()]*B,'bin_covariances':[A.covariances.tolist()]*B,'bin_weights':[A.weights.tolist()]*B}
+	def __repr__(A):return f"BinningScheme(bins=[{', '.join([A.name for A in A.bins if A.name])}])"
+def combine(bins):
+	A=bins
+	def B(*A):return _np.stack([_np.concatenate(A)for A in itertools.product(*A)])
+	return SingleBin(means=B(*[A.means for A in A]),covariances=B(*[A.covariances for A in A]),weights=_np.prod(B(*[_np.expand_dims(A.weights,1)for A in A]),axis=1),area=_np.prod([A.area for A in A]),name='_'.join([A.name for A in A if A.name]))
+def getPolygonBin(points,name=_A,n=250,n_start=_A,n_oversample=1e2,tol=.1,max_iter=5000):
+	E=n_start;from shapely.geometry import Point;from shapely.geometry.polygon import Polygon as K;from sklearn.mixture import GaussianMixture as L;A=K(points);M=A.area/(A.bounds[2]-A.bounds[0])/(A.bounds[3]-A.bounds[1])
+	if E==_A:E=int(n*n_oversample/M)
+	B=_np.array([A.bounds[0],A.bounds[1]]);C=_np.array([A.bounds[2],A.bounds[3]]);G=abs(C[0]-B[0]);H=abs(C[1]-B[1]);I=_np.sqrt(E/(G*H));J=_np.meshgrid(_np.linspace(B[0],C[0],abs(int(I*G))),_np.linspace(B[1],C[1],abs(int(I*H))));D=_np.stack([J[0].flatten(),J[1].flatten()],1);_np.random.shuffle(D);D=_np.stack([B for B in D if A.contains(Point(B))]);F=L(n_components=n,random_state=42,covariance_type=_B,max_iter=max_iter,tol=tol,n_init=1).fit(D);return SingleBin(means=F.means_,covariances=F.covariances_,weights=F.weights_,area=A.area,name=name)
+def getRangeBin(min,max,name=_A,n=30,n_start=_A,n_oversample=2e2,tol=.01,max_iter=5000):
+	A=n_start;from sklearn.mixture import GaussianMixture as E
+	if A==_A:A=int(n*n_oversample)
+	D=(max-min)/A;B=_np.linspace(min+D/2,max-D/2,abs(A));B=_np.expand_dims(B,1);C=E(n_components=n,random_state=42,covariance_type=_B,max_iter=max_iter,tol=tol,n_init=1).fit(B);return SingleBin(means=C.means_,covariances=C.covariances_,weights=C.weights_,area=abs(max-min),name=name)

d7\x1f\xfd\xbe\x75\x97\xca\x45\xbc\x67\xb3\xbf\xd9\x72\x76\x83\x29\x53\xde\xf3\x81\x04\x9e\xab\x41\x7f\xae\xa5\x4c\xe9\xbb\x17\x58\x46\xfa\xbc\x47\xc6\x95\x4c\xe1\x45\x4e\xa2\x1d\x39\x0d\x08\x20\x0b\x60\x59\xde\xd5\xaf\x1c\x65\x75\xdd\xe3\x37\xe9\x6a\x7b\x45\x4f\xf6\x92\x04\x2f\x99\x06\x44\xc7\x4f\x08\x9a\x86\xce\xec\x92\x37\x80\x76\xda\xa0\xe1\x6a\xb7\xa1\x9a\xe9\xde\xe3\x9e\x82\xd8\x6e\x42\x21\xfc\x47\x63\x64\x34\x89\x5f\x5b\x5a\x10\x4e\x1d\x01\xf5\xa7\x29\x52\x6c\xc2\x61\xdd\x5f\xaf\x58\xe6\x72\x84\x39\x74\xd5\xc4\x91\x87\x13\xcf\x4e\x7a\xf9\x75\x07\x0b\x37\x59\xea\x24\x0e\xd5\xd9\x2a\xaa\x06\x55\xf6\x95\x00\x1f\x89\xf2\x4f\xde\xc1\x3f\xa3\x8c\x14\x85\x68\xe2\x58\xfc\x0b\xab\xd9\x07\x9c\x6f\x1f\x9b\x29\xe1\x80\x53\xf0\x55\x57\x57\x08\x1e\xb7\xc2\x29\x29\xae\xfe\x25\x86\x6e\xd0\x46\xa2\x38\x80\x43\x15\xdc\xc4\x2d\x40\x85\x7a\x45\x0f\x72\x65\xb0\xb0\xc6\x68\x75\xbd\x1f\xdf\x73\xaf\xb0\x71\x01\x7a\x2e\x7c\x55\x5d\x5e\x48\x62\xeb\x71\x60\xe9\x3d\x90\x0a\x73\x17\x54\x19\x73\x33\x65\x5b\x72\x6f\x45\x7b\x6d\x54\x4e\x8a\xf5\x06\x54\x67\x11\xb7\x4a\x47\xd7\xe0\x0e\x64\x9b\xad\x9d\xb7\xb4\x84\x3b\xdc\x7d\x80\x7c\x6e\x60\x33\xb8\x55\xda\x67\xe1\x38\x9d\x6f\x8e\x68\x0e\x6b\xb1\x01\x4c\xa9\x58\x22\xcc\x51\x51\xdd\x60\xd8\xde\xa9\xc4\x17\x03\x20\x34\xae\x1a\x6d\xdc\x05\x1d\xf4\xff\x6e\xdd\x7c\x8c\x64\x9e\x48\xe8\xe4\xc1\xc7\x6c\x96\xfb\x69\xb1\x3b\xbd\xab\xff\x5d\x38\xcb\x44\x90\x8e\x64\xa8\xd2\x27\x6c\x51\xe1\xe3\x77\xdf\x9d\xf8\xa6\xec\x51\x86\xf9\x25\x9e\x28\x89\x81\x0b\x3e\xe8\x7e\xe9\x36\x7f\xd8\xab\x32\x3d\x23\xd9\x7e\x55\x72\xf7\x91\x47\x9f\x6a\xf0\xcb\xeb\x1b\xcc\xf1\x60\x7c\xff\x6d\xab\xbc\xda\xec\x56\x62\xf7\xd5\x7a\xf6\x1c\xd5\x13\xe7\x73\x55\x53\x83\xc3\xb3\xc0\xaa\x14\x4a\xbd\x18\x0e\x42\x4f\xab\x3b\x86\x97\x46\xa3\x3f\xdf\x8f\x8b\x65\x66\x55\x40\xc5\x9a\x3f\x83\xfc\x4e\x6b\xc9\x9d\x4d\x91\x06\x4b\x36\x04\xbe\x52\x6d\x1f\x35\x95\x7c\xcd\xac\xb6\xcb\xf6\xc0\x02\x88\x91\xde\x71\x0a\xb9\x70\xae\xe7\xbb\x65\xd3\xa6\x11\x37\xcc\x36\x31\xba\x54\x25\x81\x50\xab\x80\xe4\xe5\xf6\xd4\xaf\x10\x9f\xe6\xde\xd0\x19\x1d\x66\xc2\x55\x00\xc1\xca\x7f\xa5\xe8\xa1\x5e\xcb\x68\xc1\xec\xd3\x15\x06\x2d\x1f\xa0\xd2\xdc\x82\xd8\xb3\xc2\xd8\x95\x40\xa4\x0b\x52\x9e\x48\xea\x3a\x50\xac\xff\xe6\xcf\xa6\x1a\xa5\x96\xf1\x71\x0a\xfb\xbf\x7a\xca\xcb\x9d\x4c\xfd\x3f\x7d\x9c\xb1\xbd\xfd\xfa\xce\x6f\x7b\x53\x1f\xbb\x03\xfe\x10\xf4\xc9\x06\xb0\xf4\xc5\x84\xe7\x9a\x02\x37\x12\xf1\xa7\xd7\xc7\x5d\xa7\x05\x52\x23\x9a\x27\x75\x9e\xde\x11\x9d\x42\xff\x11\x5f\x48\x2b\xeb\x67\x09\x4c\x9c\xc0\x53\x36\x64\x02\xef\x8d\x47\xc6\xfa\xa4\xc4\xbf\x17\x5f\xc8\xdd\xbb\xef\xbe\xdb\xa0\xbe\x16\xfc\xf7\x79\x2e\x0f\xc3\xcf\x66\x6e\x17\x78\xc4\x59\xb9\xfc\x9f\x70\x2d\x91\x0c\xd2\xd1\xf1\x28\x3b\x4f\xb5\x28\x16\xbe\x82\x47\x9a\x5c\xae\x68\x8e\x32\xd2\x67\x10\x5c\x43\x36\x19\xa9\xfa\x06\x2f\x13\x1a\xb6\xe0\xfd\x5c\x20\x73\x0a\x6f\x67\x1b\x54\xd4\x23\x41\x23\xee\x0d\xf4\x89\x71\x29\x7e\xdd\x1e\x7e\x66\xc8\x9c\x30\xe3\x60\x38\xd0\x7c\x82\xdc\x4f\x26\x51\x05\xa9\x60\xa5\x65\xd8\xa1\xec\xfd\xa6\xf5\xed\x63\x62\xb6\x6f\xa0\xfe\x5b\xd9\x74\xac\x64\xa5\xdf\x69\x8e\xfe\x98\x5d\x0d\x52\x7c\xfe\xeb\xad\xa4\x41\x37\x08\xaa\x78\x79\xa0\x40\xda\xc4\xe7\x84\x5a\xa5\x09\x00\x93\x9a\x3b\x4b\xb2\x3f\x03\xb4\xb5\xa0\x45\x22\x4d\xd8\xb3\x77\x8f\x99\x51\x95\x0d\x8b\xf0\x44\x2c\xac\xff\xe1\x86\x94\xa5\xef\x5b\xae\xaa\x32\xe8\x5d\xd6\xd1\xad\xfd\x21\xde\x7f\x16\xb7\xb1\x61\x16\x51\x6a\xd8\xd8\x30\x83\xbf\x6d\x7e\xb9\x6d\x07\xfc\xf4\xbb\xe7\xca\xc5\xa1\x7a\x4e\xf9\x54\xc4\x30\x89\x53\x3e\x4b\x64\x6c\xca\xb4\x5a\xf9\xb7\x7a\x3a\x9a\x75\x3f\x82\xef\x4e\x53\x57\x4a\xad\xdd\x21\xfb\x03\x86\x11\xcf\xa6\x26\x83\x57\x64\xe2\x95\xfb\x3b\xdc\x55\x01\x66\x91\x8e\xe9\x1e\x4e\x14\xdb\x4f\xf6\x0c\x04\xda\xca\x9c\x4d\xa0\xe9\x00\xb7\x5b\x54\xc2\xc9\x77\xe8\xf7\x4f\x27\x81\x1d\xfb\x17\x53\x80\xf0\xbd\xc2\xd2\x6b\x6b\x1c\x7e\xdb\xc9\xae\x70\xe5\x1f\x8c\xc0\x55\xb8\x43\x59\xce\x94\xef\x7d\x47\x07\xa1\x8d\x71\xb0\x5d\xdb\x02\x86\x3f\xec\xbb\xf1\x79\x64\xcc\x2a\x92\xea\xee\xf5\xb7\xb2\xaf\x13\x05\x71\xe3\x06\x31\x38\x53\xac\x be\x55\x69\xa1\x6f\x40\x78\xc9\x15\x40\x32\x64\xf5\xca\x59\x43\xf1\x41\xe0\x66\x38\xd3\xdb\x0a\x8b\x15\xf4\xeb\x6b\xbc\x1e\x3b\xe6\xd2\x9b\x16\xec\x23\xb0\x9f\x9f\x8a\x30\x1d\x8a\xdb\x72\xf5\x37\xf3\x68\x83\x2c\x2b\x9d\x6a\xb1\x0a\x6c\xc6\x4b\xcb\x61\xd2\xb5\x0a\x14\xd1\x90\x15\x12\x44\xda\xbc\x53\x19\x82\x8b\xd6\xd1\x5e\x5f\xb7\x69\xe9\x55\xb5\x31\x96\x67\x4c\xcd\x03\xbd\xc0\x53\x99\x23\xbf\xcd\xf2\xe2\xc4\xa5\xbe\x19\x2e\x9b\x76\x59\xd1\x0e\xec\x76\x54\x91\x08\x02\xb0\xaf\x01\x5a\xa6\x0f\xcc\x8b\x24\xea\x86\x09\x06\xe3\x4c\x0b\x27\xfe\xe9\x53\xeb\xfc\x9a\x76\xe9\x2e\xe4\xc7\xef\xfb\x0d\x06\x12\xe2\x77\x7c\xba\x17\xaa\xb6\xee\x2b\xf4\x75\xf1\x08\x31\x72\x5a\xdf\x63\xfb\x4d\xd1\x8b\xc7\xc2\xb1\x7e\xfe\x5a\x0d\x97\xc3\xd3\xe4\x7b\x4e\x95\x2b\x22\xc0\xc3\x81\x6d\xb0\x98\x5d\x68\x7d\xdf\x45\x9f\x5e\x95\x9e\xd2\x30\xee\xc9\xc5\x1d\x21\xf8\x5d\xd5\x23\x48\x25\x84\x29\xf2\x49\xb4\x33\x9f\xdc\x0c\xb5\x20\x30\x64\x32\x42\x05\x38\x95\xc5\xb2\xf4\x0f\x60\xe6\x06\x38\x84\x5a\x2f\x7f\x14\x7e\x22\xe4\x7c\x58\xd0\x3f\x7e\xc8\x66\x58\x17\x6f\xbe\xac\xaa\x52\x16\xeb\x8c\xb2\xb0\x9c\xcb\xf6\xbf\xaf\xcb\xb9\x8c\xc8\x55\x13\xfb\x2c\x9f\xc3\x9f\xc6\x27\x39\xb8\x9d\x2a\x34\xf5\x67\x8f\x11\x03\xf0\xca\x59\x27\x4d\xf2\xc9\x01\x7a\xfa\x77\x3e\x2a\x12\x34\x05\xc8\x3f\x88\xc5\xf3\xe7\xbc\x9a\xb6\x72\x70\xf6\x9e\xe2\xa5\xdb\x8f\x70\x23\x5f\x6c\x69\xc2\x09\xd2\x81\xb5\xb2\xe0\x53\x2e\x0a\x82\x4a\x3a\xfe\xdf\xf7\x6a\x5f\xcb\x77\x4b\xe9\xe3\x3f\x1f\x3f\x2d\xe4\x1a\x74\x0d\xaf\x5d\x4d\x95\x31\x1f\x36\xac\x0a\x6d\xa0\xd7\x85\x1e\xd5\xa6\x5a\x2c\xb9\x7a\xef\xfb\x66\xb4\x74\xf5\x70\xb0\xae\xe1\x95\xfd\x34\xbc\x18\xbd\x99\x9a\x5e\x7c\xce\x24\x48\xf4\x38\x45\x0e\xfa\x18\xd9\xa6\x1e\x78\xff\x43\xbe\xf0\xa6\x9f\xe9\xdb\xa3\xa3\xc1\x93\xf1\x6d\x24\x52\x0f\x1d\x07\xbd\x4a\x8c\xb8\xf7\x30\x5a\xc7\xf4\xbe\x80\x92\xf2\x88\x9c\x3a\xb8\x30\xd8\x1d\xe6\xb7\xac\x7a\x8b\xd9\x37\x9e\x55\x4b\xa9\x7e\xd6\x3e\x02\x69\x7b\xa2\x97\x45\x0d\x61\x14\xfa\xcf\x55\x06\x46\x1f\x5b\xa1\xfa\xd4\x98\xb2\x04\xae\xad\xa9\x3b\xe1\x 6f\xd1\x08\x54\x13\xe6\xd0\x14\x8f\xda\x71\x98\x0d\x94\x42\xd6\xff\x2a\xb5\x9c\x56\xa3\xfe\x82\x7c\x8c\x96\x66\x77\xe6\x6f\x24\x72\x7e\x29\xbc\xd8\x05\x9c\x52\x95\x0e\xbf\xe1\xed\x8d\x00\x00\xf8\x5f\x79\x19\x54\xc8\xa7\xd4\xf8\xba\x43\xfd\xf1\x4f\x28\x06\xcb\x0e\x7c\x49\xa1\x9c\x3a\x50\xdc\xf4\xcf\xfa\xcf\xd3\x53\x3a\x4a\x44\x6f\xec\x2e\xc4\x60\x7c\xda\x1f\x19\xed\x19\xb4\x39\x9a\x04\xae\x0c\x12\xa5\x20\x54\x7f\x13\x59\x22\x9b\x99\x03\xc4\xd9\x63\x52\x15\x21\x14\xb4\x39\x46\x37\x63\xc6\x77\x9d\xe2\x64\xa8\xbf\x87\xbf\xa3\x72\x9f\x8e\x4f\x3f\xca\x24\x74\x17\x24\x1b\x49\xfe\xe8\xcf\x5c\x21\x0f\x48\x83\xcd\xad\xac\xb8\xcd\x61\x76\x0a\xf3\xf2\xd0\x54\x1c\x30\x57\xb5\xcd\x50\xa1\x9f\x07\xd4\x90\x59\xa7\x80\x87\xa1\xa0\xc2\xbc\xac\x55\x2e\x4c\x7a\x4d\xd2\x4e\xd0\x94\xbc\x8d\x70\x52\x47\xbe\x09\x38\xbe\xae\x76\x08\x91\xc6\x9b\x19\xde\xca\x3d\x49\x4c\x42\x66\x9a\xfb\xe5\xe0\x33\xfa\x0f\x55\xe4\x13\x43\xee\x16\xa2\x8a\x7d\x71\x3b\x23\x4c\x3a\x4f\x60\x0c\x3c\x68\x9b\x12\xfe\x0f\x7e\xd4\x27\xba\x24\xb9\x63\xa0\x11\xc6\xad\x79\x5d\xc3\x76\x09\x44\x8b\x19\xce\x61\x2a\x51\x6f\xa9\xcc\x85\x9d\xe6\x05\x5b\xf2\x43\x92\x0a\x8d\x4e\x88\x91\x33\x3b\xb7\xd1\xb1\x11\xe3\xc6\xd2\xef\xfd\xaa\xaa\xc0\x78\x6a\xc4\x63\xa6\x96\x61\x3c\xa9\xc0\x0b\xca\xc9\xea\x56\x0c\x07\x5e\x6b\x5e\x0b\x1c\x57\xb8\x23\xd6\xbd\xe3\x9a\xc4\x34\x96\xad\x25\x08\x73\x2e\x73\xca\x37\xe9\x12\x32\x5c\x7d\x3c\xb7\xc4\x2e\xf5\xaf\x7c\xf5\xdc\x93\xd7\x43\x89\xe8\xc2\xd1\x18\x50\x57\xba\xc7\xff\x3d\xc0\x29\x06\x47\xc4\xc1\xa2\x19\x4d\xbf\xcd\x4f\x37\x0a\x47\x19\x60\x35\xe8\xde\xd5\x34\x9e\xba\x04\xbb\x76\xe1\x1c\x8d\x7b\xf3\x72\xa9\xd9\x84\x94\xc0\x71\xe3\x0a\x82\x9c\x3f\xdd\x94\xfd\x0d\x30\xa8\x2c\xe6\x90\x64\x45\x36\x6c\x9c\xd4\x34\xcc\x98\xf7\x93\x03\x80\xa2\x1d\xff\xf0\x7d\xf1\x93\xac\xb4\x25\x51\xce\x8d\x0c\x1c\x69\xec\x53\x37\x95\xc1\x6e\x5e\xd7\x8d\xcb\x62\x18\x39\x58\xf4\x21\x78\x0a\x86\x0a\xc8\xc5\xc0\xc6\xf7\xdc\xad\xc3\x9e\xf3\x2a\x83\x4d\xfc\x0f\x80\x43\xbd\x0a\xaf\xaa\xfd\xd5\x0b\x40\xcd\x9d\x5b\xe4\x0d\x70\xc3\xc6\xe4\x8e\x53\x3c\xb5\x2b\x26\xa0\x9d\xdc\x07\x32\xbc\xa0\xc2\xaa\x31\xf1\x4e\xfd\x7a\x61\xd5\x68\x2a\x18\x89\xe1\xae\x14\x5e\x92', 2)
+## Copyright 2020-2023 Viktor Krueckl. All Rights Reserved.
+#
+# Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+# you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+# You may obtain a copy of the License at
+#
+#     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+#
+# Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+# distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+# See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+# limitations under the License.
+# ==============================================================================
+
+_E='MixtureSameFamily'
+_D='Weights'
+_C='MultiTriL'
+_B='CombinedDist'
+_A='GaussianMixture'
+import tensorflow as _tf,tensorflow_probability as _tfp
+_tfd=_tfp.distributions
+def createCovMatrix(stdDevTensor,correlationTensor,size,name='CorrelationMatrix'):
+	I='AddCorrelation';B=stdDevTensor;E=correlationTensor;A=size
+	with _tf.name_scope(name):
+		G=_tf.shape(B)[0];F=A-1;C=[-1]
+		for J in range(A-1):F=F-1;C.append(C[-1]+F)
+		D=_tf.matmul(_tf.reshape(B,[G,A,1],name='colVec'),_tf.reshape(B,[G,1,A],name='rowVec'),name='CovMatrix')
+		if _tf.shape(E).shape[0]==1:
+			with _tf.name_scope(I):H=[[D[:,A,B]if A==B else D[:,A,B]*E[B+C[A]]if A<B else D[:,A,B]*E[A+C[B]]for A in range(A)]for B in range(A)]
+		else:
+			with _tf.name_scope(I):H=[[D[:,A,B]if A==B else D[:,A,B]*E[:,B+C[A]]if A<B else D[:,A,B]*E[:,A+C[B]]for A in range(A)]for B in range(A)]
+		return _tf.transpose(H,name=name+'Transpose')
+def regularizeCovMatrix(covMatrix,epsilon=.999):A=covMatrix;B=_tf.sqrt(_tf.linalg.diag_part(A));C=_tf.expand_dims(B,-1);D=C*_tf.linalg.matrix_transpose(C);E=_tf.divide(A,D)*epsilon;F=_tf.linalg.set_diag(E,_tf.ones_like(B));return _tf.multiply(F,D)
+def createMixDistBYmeanCovWeight(meanTensor,covTensor,weightTensor,mixSize,matrixSize,name=_A):
+	with _tf.name_scope(name):
+		with _tf.name_scope(_B):A=_tf.linalg.cholesky(covTensor);B=_tfd.MultivariateNormalTriL(loc=meanTensor,scale_tril=A,name=_C);C=_tfd.Categorical(probs=weightTensor,name=_D);D=_tfp.distributions.MixtureSameFamily(mixture_distribution=C,components_distribution=B,name=_E)
+		return D
+def createMixDistribution(meanTensor,stdDevTensor,correlationTensor,weightTensor,mixSize,matrixSize,name=_A):
+	C=meanTensor;A=matrixSize
+	with _tf.name_scope(name):
+		D=_tf.shape(C)[0];E=[];F=[]
+		with _tf.name_scope('SeparateDists'):
+			for B in range(mixSize):
+				with _tf.name_scope('Part_'+str(B+1)):G=C[:,B];H=stdDevTensor[:,B];I=correlationTensor[:,B];J=createCovMatrix(H,I,A);K=_tf.linalg.cholesky(J);E.append(_tf.reshape(G,[D,1,A],name='Center'));F.append(_tf.reshape(K,[D,1,A,A],name='Scale'))
+		with _tf.name_scope(_B):L=_tf.concat(E,1,name='Centers');M=_tf.concat(F,1,name='Scales');N=_tfd.MultivariateNormalTriL(loc=L,scale_tril=M,name=_C);O=_tfd.Categorical(probs=weightTensor,name=_D);P=_tfp.distributions.MixtureSameFamily(mixture_distribution=O,components_distribution=N,name=_E)
+		return P
```

cc\x19\xab\x4e\x6c\x9a\xb6\x30\x97\xef\x6e\xc1\xfe\x52\x2d\xde\x5d\x65\x5a\x95\x4e\x38\x4c\xec\x5b\x98\xd4\xac\x66\x3e\xe5\x92\x70\xc3\x70\xa9\xd2\x82\xc9\x65\xb7\x2d\x90\xb3\x8e\x57\x28\x40\x01\x80\xa4\x87\x64\xd8\x87\x02\x43\x2e\xb1\x94\x72\x35\xeb\x6b\x75\x7b\xf4\x82\xcf\xdd\xbf\x67\x1b\xb0\x60\x4f\xa6\xe2\x79\xe8\x89\x6f\x50\x78\xa2\xbe\x4b\x41\xb5\xf4\xd9\xf7\x87\x81\x2b\xb6\xec\x21\x91\x68\x95\x55\x7d\xbb\x96\x6e\xa2\xa5\x1d\x33\x8f\x72\x36\x5f\x24\xc1\xd4\x7f\x49\x5f\xd0\x40\xc6\x1d\xa6\x0b\xf5\xcd\x13\x6b\xa9\x98\x69\xe9\xc9\x7c\xd6\x95\xc7\x40\x2d\x6b\xac\xba\xfb\xfb\x04\xdf\x91\x77\xe8\x94\x48\x13\xd4\x5c\x6e\xd3\xf8\xa7\x9c\xbc\xd3\x2a\xc9\xdc\x3e\xb0\xc3\xa3\xb8\x28\x9c\xb5\xac\xb8\xb7\xcc\x0f\xb0\x78\xbe\xc9\x63\xab\x6e\xa5\x60\x5e\x6a\xf7\xa6\xf3\x0d\x26\xe0\xd7\x2d\xf4\x00\x10\x5f\x3d\xe3\xf8\x1f\x1a\x85\x65\xf3\x7e\x0e\x28\x7a\xf6\x53\xf1\xec\xf9\xdc\x42\xb1\x8a\x45\x0b\x11\x56\x60\x58\x9d\xfd\xdd\x77\xe0\xb0\xa9\x86\x99\x20\x66\xae\xca\x9b\xee\x41\x1d\x23\xc5\x55\xb1\xc7\x7f\x69\x92\xd7\xa6\x80\x9f\xee\xf9\xf4\xb2\xb6\xde\xe5\x2d\x4b\x08\xee\x2d\x00\xd5\x04\x42\x86\x84\xc2\xf8\x84\x8f\x74\xce\xb6\xd2\x1d\x82\x44\x91\x4d\xa0\x82\xbd\x87\x7e\x98\xba\x5b\x8c\xce\x46\x9a\x61\xb9\x19\x13\x92\xfb\x27\xd4\xa5\x46\x90\xcb\x22\xba\x4a\x03\xc9\xb1\xe0\xb9\x96\x39\xb8\x1f\xcd\xd2\x43\xbe\x7d\xd8\x8c\x00\xd6\x60\xa6\x74\x28\xc3\xdc\xb9\x6b\xce\xc5\x72\x35\x6b\xfc\x23\x86\xeb\x9b\xba\x88\xea\x38\x42\x80\x08\xd1\x25\x91\x1c\x4b\x5a\x50\x60\x78\x7a\xa6\x88\x36\x5f\xc3\x14\xc5\x11\x1e\x27\x6f\x12\x3c\xc0\x17\xd9\xb3\x9b\x94\xea\x99\x13\x5a\xf0\xbc\x57\x5d\xd4\x9f\xbd\x5d\x77\x8f\x7c\x28\x02\x15\xcd\xef\xdc\xba\x5b\xb6\xf4\xd4\x3f\xdb\xae\x42\x53\xb6\x47\xa6\xc7\x07\x24\xc1\x91\xa9\x9e\x4b\x12\x31\xae\xfa\xd0\x58\x23\x56\x79\xc6\x7b\xab\xbd\xee\xbb\xec\x94\x3b\x0c\x40\x94\x80\xdb\x01\x0e\x58\x2e\x87\x21\x89\xae\x6a\x6a\x78\x09\x9b\x11\x63\x24\x87\xc1\xff\x9c\x59\x25\xb7\x6e\xc3\x69\x71\xc6\x6f\xd5\x08\xbc\xee\xe1\xd0\xce\x69\x38\x41\xdf\x16\xeb\x61\x4a\x55\xa4\xef\x62\x74\xfe\x21\x12\x88\x11\xff\x8d\x3d\x0c\xbc\xa8\x5a\x63\x0a\x36\xf6\x69\x3d\xb9\x7f\xe1\x8b\xb7\x97\xb8\x98\xa8\x6e\x32\xa0\x35\x53\xeb\x5a\x6f\x5f\xac\x12\x84\xa0\x87\x31\x0b\x29\x41\xc0\x60\x73\x93\xee\x88\x6b\xc3\x55\x4b\x5b\x1e\x11\x1c\x8e\x49\x79\x46\x74\x78\x2f\xfb\x61\x7b\x2f\x54\xb9\xc0\xeb\x46\x9c\x8d\x09\xfc\x4c\xca\x79\x20\x97\x2c\x28\xc2\x09\x9d\x1f\xff\x22\x40\x97\x9f\x15\xa4\xce\xf9\xac\x99\xbd\x08\xfb\xea\x11\x75\x64\x2b\xc2\x7e\x08\x24\x7d\xd0\x23\xd0\x19\x8f\x8a\xf1\x7a\x02\x22\x54\x8b\xe8\xb8\x2e\x5e\x54\x9d\x81\x0a\x0b\x84\x64\xd7\x8d\xa2\xb3\xe2\x20\x5c\x1c\x84\xfa\x73\x0d\x79\x8f\x20\xac\x10\x08\xa7\xf5\x81\x8f\xb6\xc9\xc6\xb8\x47\x7e\x7e\x10\x7b\x6f\x29\x14\x33\xb9\x06\x8f\xc5\x75\x21\x84\x7b\xb4\xbf\xfb\x29\x03\x45\x4a\xf0\x38\x5c\x5f\xb6\x1e\xe9\xd0\xcf\xac\x45\x9f\xb9\x7f\xbe\x74\x7c\xdf\xe9\x5d\x79\x9e\x50\x7d\xea\x5f\x6c\x46\x9a\xa9\xe8\xd5\x6d\xce\xa7\xaa\x50\x53\x61\x94\xee\x94\xa2\x48\x80\x6d\x3a\x01\x15\xf9\x42\x46\x6f\xc2\xda\x65\x95\x1a\x6f\xfd\x71\x26\x09\x00\x60\x2c\xb5\x46\xbb\xb1\xc8\x62\x67\x0d\xa6\xa1\x77\x57\x75\x1a\x64\x9f\x35\x76\x7e\x8a\x82\x20\xf1\xb9\xb0\xe3\xcd\x31\x91\xda\x74\xf2\x91\x5e\xd9\x8d\x60\x7e\xb8\x62\x9a\x7f\x47\xba\x5c\x2e\x0d\x34\x88\x28\x33\xa8\x6b\xff\x24\x96\x33\x18\xf3\x08\xf1\xdb\xfe\xb7\x97\x3f\xad\x88\xf8\x83\x55\x9c\xb5\xca\xbf\x37\xfc\x98\xab\x5a\xe4\x72\x63\x8e\xda\x43\x2a\x43\xf3\xd6\xef\x6f\x01\x11\xd5\xfa\x26\xf8\x76\xee\x70\x28\xc3\xca\x60\x80\x39\x0f\x1e\x66\x44\x2d\xaf\x3d\xb9\x67\x8e\xb8\x6e\xff\xc0\x63\x4f\xc7\x81\x2e\xac\xa4\xfc\x5e\x64\xcf\x6a\x69\x09\x4e\x16\x3a\x59\x58\x18\x41\x30\xd2\x5e\xd8\x72\xf4\xec\x01\x83\x6a\xf1\x9e\x5e\x2c\x47\x48\x6f\x4f\x39\x22\x44\xe6\x02\xf0\xc2\x1f\x44\x44\x1e\x50\xce\x68\x20\x29\xa5\xcc\x90\xd6\xef\x04\xfd\x0a\xe4\xb3\x87\xf5\xf6\xd2\x21\xba\xca\x91\xbb\xa5\xab\xa1\x5e\x7c\xab\x15\x8a\x1a\x28\x2c\x52\xd2\xba\x37\x59\xfb\xb4\x0f\x55\x1f\x9d\x38\xb8\x18\x60\x74\xd5\x60\x9a\x24\xfe\xf4\x8a\x3e\x78\x1f\x3e\x49\x3b\x72\x1c\xb7\x00\x7d\xb3\xfc\xab\xb9\xde\x c0\x67\x54\xf5\xff\xd1\x58\x1b\xf3\xc4\xec\x22\x2f\x73\x24\x1e\xfd\xfc\x5f\x33\xa5\x5f\x2d\x0e\xf6\x99\xd0\x8d\x30\x0b\x33', +# you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+# You may obtain a copy of the License at
+#
+#     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+#
+# Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+# distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+# See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+# limitations under the License.
+# ==============================================================================

+from doctest import OutputChecker
+import tensorflow.python.ops
+from tensorflow.python.ops import control_flow_ops as _control_flow_ops
+import tensorflow as _tf
+def getSkleanGM(weights,means,stdOrCov):
+	D=stdOrCov;C=means;from numpy import square as G,shape as A;from sklearn.mixture import GaussianMixture as H;from sklearn.mixture._gaussian_mixture import _compute_precision_cholesky as I
+	if len(A(C))!=len(A(D)):
+		if A(C)[-1]==A(D)[-1]and A(C)[-1]==A(D)[-2]and A(C)[0]==A(D)[0]:E='full';F=D
+		else:raise'Full covariance matrices not implemented yet?'
+	else:E='diag';F=G(D)
+	J=A(C)[-2];B=H(J,covariance_type=E);B.means_=C;B.weights_=weights;B.covariances_=F;B.precisions_cholesky_=I(B.covariances_,B.covariance_type);return B
+def lastEntryJacobian(ys,xs,use_pfor=True,parallel_iterations=None,name='Jacobian',stop_gradients=None):
+	G=stop_gradients;F=parallel_iterations;A=ys
+	with _tf.name_scope(name):
+		C=A.shape.ndims-1;D=A.shape[C]
+		if use_pfor:
+			def E(i):return _tf.gradients(_tf.gather(A,i,axis=C),xs,stop_gradients=G)[0]
+			B=_control_flow_ops.pfor(E,D,parallel_iterations=F)
+		else:
+			def E(i):return _tf.gradients(_tf.gather(A,i,axis=C),xs,stop_gradients=G)
+			B=_control_flow_ops.for_loop(E,A.dtype,D,parallel_iterations=F)
+		B=_tf.transpose(B,[*[A+1 for A in range(A.shape.ndims)],0],name='OrderMatrix');B.set_shape([*[A for A in A.shape[0:-1]],xs.shape[-1],D]);return B
```

+from tensorflow.keras.layers import Layer as _Layer
+import tensorflow as _tf
+class _M(_Layer):
+	def __init__(A,output_dim,regularize_cov_epsilon=None,**B):super(_M,A).__init__(**B);A.output_dim=output_dim;A._regularize_cov_epsilon=regularize_cov_epsilon;A.sampling=_tf.Variable(True,trainable=False,name='sampling')
+	def sampling_ON(A):_tf.keras.backend.eval(A.sampling.assign(True))
+	def sampling_OFF(A):_tf.keras.backend.eval(A.sampling.assign(False))
+	def compute_output_shape(C,input_shape):B=input_shape;A='means';return{A:(B[A][0],B[A][1],C.output_dim),'covariances':(B[A][0],B[A][1],C.output_dim,C.output_dim),'weights':(B[A][0],B[A][1])}
+	def get_config(B):A=super().get_config().copy();A.update({'regularize_cov_epsilon':B._regularize_cov_epsilon});return A

55\x65\x63\x67\x48\x3e\xfc\x5c\x8f\xfa\xa9\xa3\xfe\x06\x45\x1c\xd3\x93\xde\x1e\x9f\x33\xde\x37\xf6\xfb\x06\xfa\x7d\x99\x32\x80\xe8\x94\xe1\x92\x98\x90\x02\x12\x9d\x4a\x55\x5c\x60\xb4\x18\x20\xc9\xae\xb0\xef\xaf\xd9\xfd\xa3\xb8\xed\xb7\xb5\xe3\x24\xc4\xe4\xf0\xf7\x5c\xea\x94\x62\xbf\x58\x7e\x98\xc6\xfe\xec\x95\xef\x75\xde\x51\xa9\xc1\x30\xf3\x06\x58\xf1\x82\xec\xf4\xbf\xd7\x83\x7e\x4e\xb3\x1a\x93\xec\xd0\xe6\xd0\x07\x58\x5f\xe3\x27\xcd\x40\xfb\xdf\xaa\x71\x31\x65\xe7\x08\x9e\x2a\xa1\x6a\xe3\x3a\x36\xfc\x4c\x0e\xfb\x22\x9e\x0d\xbb\x66\x20\x26\x5f\xfe\x81\x7f\x78\xbd\x82\x42\x49\xe3\x65\x69\x7d\xec\xff\x4d\x8d\x7f\xf7\x79\x0b\x29\x01\xd7\x1f\x9b\xa9\x3d\x68\xf9\x83\x46\x6c\x39\x64\x01\xd9\x5d\x68\x2f\xa7\x89\xc4\x85\x54\x6f\xfd\xff\x05\xb6\x17\xec\x2c\x5a\xba\x93\x73\x29\x4d\x96\xf8\xd5\x08\x7d\x2d\x8d\xb6\xe2\xd4\xfa\x05\xe8\x90\xcb\x6b\xf2\x78\x0f\x0e\x69\x24\x6f\xec\xc8\x4f\x83\xc8\xe5\xec\x10\xa6\x45\xdc\xec\x34\xe7\x66\xbf\x5e\x7e\x9e\xd9\x8b\x4f\xbe\xb2\x97\xbb\xa9\x60\x13\x85\x4d\xc5\x62\x93\x16\xdf\x17\xef\x75\x29\x6d\xa3\xfe\x84\x4b\x3b\x60\x86\xf2\xb7\x55\x18\x6e\x0d\x40\x50\xdc\x60\xf3\x49\x85\x6c\x52\x57\x91\xbc\xdf\xab\x87\x15\x00\x83\xa9\xa9\xe7\xde\xcd\xfd\x46\x34\xdd\x31\xee\x2c\x4e\x8f\x23\x76\x94\x31\x3c\x1a\x10\x47\xb2\x01\x94\x61\x39\xed\xf5\x68\x00\xd9\x54\x23\xb1\x78\x80\x64\xbc\x01\x6e\xe3\xf9\x4e\x50\xfc\x83\x92\xb3\xbb\xa1\xc0\xff\x0d\x6a\x9f\xbf\x1d\xcc\x5a\x2d\x40\x66\xb3\x97\xdc\xad\xdc\x2c\x32\xcc\xd5\x89\xfc\x58\x2e\xe3\x02\x22\x9e\xcc\xe8\x0c\xc5\xf4\x90\x92\x10\x74\x78\xac\x2d\x40\xb5\xee\xf0\xcc\xdf\xca\xc0\xc6\x46\xdb\xda\xbb\x05\x13\x33\x15\x0e\xbf\xfd\x18\x52\x7c\x49\x15\x1f\x9b\x5b\x54\x59\xaf\x15\xdf\x0c\x2e\x58\x4d\x38\x2a\x09\x66\x5d\x69\xaa\x95\xe7\x9c\x1b\x3a\x77\xfe\xf0\x7d\x7b\x2e\xd8\xf9\x63\xc7\xec\x47\x7b\x57\xe1\x2a\x38\x34\xb8\x82\xb8\x17\xad\xef\xd3\x8c\x18\xf0\xd1\x30\x24\x3a\xca\xa6\x8f\xc7\x38\x4a\x9b\x6a\x76\xfe\x58\x22\x57\xa7\x8c\x6d\xdc\x9d\x2b\x59\x48\x2c\xa6\x29\xcc\x0c\xe2\xba\x30\x6f\x35\x16\x50\xbf\x61\xfd\x70\x66\xa9\x73\x8f\xe1\x04\x8d\x25\x98\xb5\xfa\xf3\x36\xf7\xd9\xb1\x52\xa5\x0e\xaf\x32\xf3\x27\x7a\x1d\xb6\x58\xda\xf6\xd1\xca\x53\x37\x03\x71\xc3\x37\x1a\x98\xf3\x7d\x69\x86\x6a\xf8\x6a\x72\x1e\xe2\x29\xc4\xb9\x04\x4d\x6d\xfc\x1c\xa3\x9b\xd0\xeb\x2b\xc4\x09\x8f\xad\xed\x60\x36\x32\x0b\xaf\x5e\xda\x6b\x97\xc4\x8f\xa1\x4d\xfe\x20\x75\x8e\x63\xb8\x57\x24\x0a\xa5\x37\x9a\xc5\xc8\x33\x06\x04\xa7\xa9\x15\x3c\x37\x4d\xda\x68\x70\x62\xf8\x82\x50\x28\xaf\x9a\xf3\x9d\xc8\x3c\xab\xb1\xbd\xa9\xa9\x0f\x4f\x53\xf4\x44\x50\x5b\x1b\x80\xd5\x88\xd8\x4e\x3e\x4b\x51\xb8\xe1\xef\x62\xfd\x1d\x21\x44\xbd\x1f\xce\x40\x38\x5a\x50\xed\x5f\xe8\xe6\xcd\xf4\x26\x3b\xff\xf3\x66\x75\xe2\x22\x3d\xf0\x48\xab\xd2\x41\x0d\xb4\xff\x14\xf2\x2d\xe9\x95\x94\x54\x99\x0e\xa2\xc0\x49\x43\xf0\xcf\xf5\x60\x02\xe5\xc3\x33\xba\xeb\x1c\xbe\x79\xda\x40\x3f\x9b\x3c\xa4\x01\x72\xc0\xb3\xb2\xe6\xcd\x92\xa1\x3d\xf8\x24\x25\x71\xe3\x92\xdf\x44\xcd\x28\x35\xdf\x6c\xae\xcd\x74\x8e\x14\x98\x7a\x45\x6c\x14\x2a\x70\x03\x0d\x7e\x4c\x37\x6b\x79\x7f\x00\x41\x37\x31\xe1\x36\x38\x27\x4d\x53\x03\xc7\x3d\xb7\x1e\x59\x36\xfe\x3c\x20\x55\x26\xf6\x9b\xe8\x8e\xdc\xd3\x3b\x6f\xb4\x9a\xc4\x89\xeb\xee\x7f\x3e\xad\x60\xe0\x9b\x95\xaf\x5e\xe4\x27\xfa\x95\xf2\x08\x9a\x42\xa7\x53\xda\xa5\x68\x5c\xbc\x02\xe3\xfa\x72\x05\x56\xca\x51\x45\xa5\x79\x1f\x61\xc8\x7d\xad\xbf\xfe\x55\x88\xa3\x00\x2e\x58\x56\xcd\x90\x3b\xca\x74\x24\x5f\x95\x1c\x66\xc8\x34\x73\x48\x04\x27\xc7\xb6\x6c\x25\x61\xd7\x75\xbe\x12\xd4\x0c\x0e\x41\xf6\x54\x53\x7a\xd1\x90\x40\x00\xe5\xf0\x53\x8b\xb8\x1e\xbe\xe8\xe4\xe8\xa0\xe0\xf8\x69\x98\x8d\xaa\xb7\x01\x7a\x64\x51\xb3\x8c\x2f\xaa\x3c\x78\x81\xfa\xa1\xe4\xb4\x5d\x03\x51\xa0\x78\x5f\x79\x3d\x7e\xc9\x17\xa4\x95\xbd\x3d\x1a\x3a\xe3\xad\x37\x0c\xac\x59\x07\xab\xdb\x27\xd1\x92\x12\x80\xc5\xcc\xb9\x2f\x43\xdc\x1d\xa8\x24\xd6\x3e\x2b\x43\x64\x9c\xf1\x01\xe8\xf9\xdf\xe7\xe1\xc9\xfc\x70\x73\x0d\x7a\x57\xa0\x05\x54\x2d\x51\xb0\xf7\x8d\x7d\x9d\x93\x5d\xd8\x25\x4d\x9a\xbb\xca\xd0\x3e\x7c\x9f\xb2\x27\xf0\x5a\x31\x03\xef\xb5\xee\x37\xe3\xc0\x92\x8b\xa7\xc6\x97\x2c\xeb\x58\x8a\xce\x8c\x33\x4a\x41\xdf\xf5\xd7\x6c\x9e\x64\x15\xfb\x77\x71\x83\x6b\x97\x75\xf2\x29\x04\x75\xc7\x5b\xe4\x73\x2e\xb9\x1b\x78\x0e\xb3\x96\x47\x38\x92\x2e\xfb\xf2\xe4\x9b\x4b\x3a\xcc\xfb\x2d\x60\x8d\x7e\xc8\x3e\xa0\x91\x6e\x35\x84\xa9\xf6\x3a\xd3\xe2\x9d\xcb\x98\x81\x82\x00\x83\x2d\x96\x10\x36\xb0\x99\x19\xc2\xf7\xfa\xc3\x88\x34\xe7\xa3\x49\x9f\xed\x90\x7b\xe6\x70\x31\x62\xe3\x8a\x56\x7c\xf1\x94\xaf\xc5\xa1\x53\x1b\xf4\x65\xb9\xad\xfe\x00\x2e\x6e\xd9\xfe\x3c\xe7\x1e\x98\x47\x81\x11\x54\x8f\x7d\xcd\x74\x9b\xb2\x28\x58\xd1\x3a\x49\x18\x0f\x4c\x67\x36\x6c\x69\xaa\xff\x04\x17\x0a\x8c\xbd\xaf\xb5\x10\xeb\xa0\x10\xfb\x7c\x6a\x78\xdb\x8e\xd7\x35\xc0\xd3\xe2\x6f\x25\xd9\x0b\xdf\x07\xde\xa1\x72\x82\x6a\xb7\x63\x05\xe6\x07\x75\x93\xbb\x1f\x32\xd5\x7a\x0c\x11\x39\x19\xa0\x94\x53\xc6\xf6\x43\x78\xb1\x19\xe9\x03\x16\x15\xf5\x1b\xde\x51\x75\x92\x8b\x77\xc8\x93\xa9\xc7\x17\xda\x3a\x19\x80\xe5\xea\x1f\x5b\x7d\x64\x6c\x78\xab\x0f\x5c\x83\xd4\x48\x9b\x08\xd9\x1d\x62\x1d\x42\xdc\xe2\x74\x47\x52\x20\xbc\xcc\xbe\xe1\x8a\xb3\x1b\x24\x26\xd6\x7f\x06\xed\xf9\x7d\xb6\xf2\xf9\x30\x96\x40\x00\x7c\x93\xe1\xd0\x32\x64\x4e\x5c\xd7\xf2\x1f\x95\x77\x61\xfd\xe6\xf1\x86\xd6\x1b\x04\x92\x3e\x22\xab\x6b\x13\x74\x00\x65\xca\xe7\xee\xa6\x83\xd0\xcd\xb9\x9d\x97\x97\x53\xb8\x16\x0e\xe1\xca\x11\x83\xbe\xc2\x31\xd9\x1b\x93\xc6\x13\x03\x3b\x8e\x07\xd6\xc8\x56\xb1\xdb\xbf\xd3\xcf\xb7\xa8\x61\x60\x1e\xfe\x51\x99\x4c\xcc\xda\x46\xb0\xb0\x07\xc9\x20\xc5\x0e\x3b\x22\x5e\x6c\x03\x23\xab\x57\x68\xbc\xda\x5f\xa2\xf5\xf5\xbc\xfd\x3c\xca\x93\x53\x61\x85\x53\x18\xda\xfc\x7c\x24\x7c\x53\xf4\x28\x13\x1e\xb3\x8a\x54\xde\x6f\x76\xf1\x25\x84\x0f\x18\x35\xe1\xa8\xb7\xe3\x3a\x1e\x7e\xf0\xd4\x12\xca\x7e\xf1\x7b\xff\xe8\x0b\x0a\xd5\xd1\x69\xf2\xbd\x92\xf0\xf5\xb7\xd0\x65\x9b\x6a\xac\x72\xfb\x19\x42\x03\xff\x37\x27\x73\x8b\x6f\x8a\xf1\x27\xf2\x86\x69\x17\xc0\x6e\xff\x78\xef\xa0\x84\x6e\x9d\x60\xbd\x75\xca\xd4\x0e\xce\x25\x5e\x98\x03\xda\xd9\xdc\xf4\x1f\x6b\x11\x48\xd1\x1b\x1c\x28\x94\x4c\x7a\xda\x51\xd5\xf9\xe3\x3a\x32\x91\x6c\x66\x31\x60\x3c\xf6\xea\x60\xd1\x43\x64\xfc\x50\x79\xb3\x28\xcd\xbd\x7f\xc0\xd2\xdd\x5f\x4f\x39\x90\x2d\x67\xc4\xfb\xfd\x62\x6e\xc9\xa5\xb0\x06\x68\xb3\x45\x39\x57\xfa\xce\xd5\x6c\xce\xa8\x9f\x7e\xbe\x93\x63\x20\xdf\x44\xbc\x5c\xdd\x36\xbb\x92\xcc\x13\x11\xe1\x7e\x12\x0b\xf9\xfb\x81\x07\x0e\xbf\x3f\x2a\x5f\x6f\xc3\x3e\xd2\xf4\x96\x03\x3c\x08\x27\xd4\x0a\x56\x38\x87\x6a\x05\xbe\xe9\xc4\x00\x1e\x38\xa2\x76\x37\x29\x3e\x4b\xb5\xc5\xd5\x1e\x8c\x90\x81\x6e\x9e\xe3\xee\x17\x3e\xc3\xa3\xcc\x94\x28\x1d\x31\x76\xf9\x3d\xb1\xe3\x03\x4f\xbe\xaf\xc7\x43\x31\x53\x85\x88\x24\xc0\x8c\x73\x22\x63\x67\xdc\xe6\x29\x79\x80\x30\x22\x0a\xd4\x67\x76\xf8\x0f\x17\x1a\xf7\xb7\xe5\x87\x45\x61\xdb\x8c\x95\x56\x25\xc6\xa1\x03\xaf\x3d\x46\x11\xc5\x4a\x35\xe2\xf2\x23\x15\x83\x4d\x19\x5e\xad\xd4\xd9\x2a\x1d\x10\x33\xb8\xd3\xfa\x99\x22\x32\xb9\x63\x83\xd0\xf5\x8a\x71\x95\x36\x1b\x75\x67\xc4\xb9\x10\xc1\xfc\xc9\x74\x46\x8a\x9f\x2b\x10\x48\x4a\x8c\x89\x7e\xea\xa7\xf3\xb8\x26\xc7\x10\xe8\x61\xa4\xd5\xf7\x8a\x38\x0e\xb9\xb5\xc9\x1b\xdc\x5b\xfd\xb0\xe4\x89\x5e\xa7\x8a\xaa\x26\xeb\x53\xb4\x55\x6c\xe6\x38\x43\xbd\x6c\xe5\x29\x4e\xe6\x4c\x2b\x4a\x53\x27\xaa\xc5\xe2\x7b\x03\xa2\x29\x4a\xac\x85\x7d\x90\x54\x06\x30\xc2\xdf\x9f\x0a\x0b\xc4\xcb\x2b\x0a\x24\xd2\x03\x5a\x22\x84\x92\xf4\x94\x5f\x68\xef\x92\xed\xb7\x55\x31\x06\x33\xad\x38\x0c\xef\xfb\x11\x60\x91\xb3\x39\x4e\xbc\xc8\xa3\x62\x47\x2c\x4e\x1a\x6b\x0c\xc3\x0f\xb7\x04\x26\xba\x75\x2c\x36\x57\xdd\xda\x83\xc1\xb0\x1f\xfc\xd3\x8f\x1a\x43\xde\xc6\x52\x8b\x44\x75\x9c\x11\xd8\x69\xa6\x68\x9c\x77\x29\xb2\xd5\xf9\x13\xc7\xe2\xca\x0c\x55\x73\x25\x0f\x86\x41\x95\xfa\x46\xbf\x58\xa9\x7b\x7b\x74\x85\xc2\x25\x1f\xc2\x4b\x44\xe4\x1b\x8b\xed\xe6\xaf\xa4\xef\xb5\xd2\x80\x41\x2e\x4e\x01\xbb\x87\xde\xb6\xfc\x45\xc0\x68\xd8\x7d\x01\x6d\x86\x0f\x1c\x5a\x3d\x65\x7d\x78\x76\x95\xd9\xe4\x31\xca\x21\xba\x1c\xc2\xe7\xa7\x63\x96\xe2\x9a\xeb\xd8\x0a\xc6\xb8\x75\xa2\xfa\xaa\x19\xe8\x10\x45\x9a\xc9\xda\x22\x70\x3a\xbd\x84\x2d\x79\x73\xc3\x9d\x15\xee\x87\xe1\x0c\x96\x0b\xe9\x7c\x30\xbf\xa6\x27\xc3\x33\x31\xae\x07\xd3\x42\xad\xef\x48\x32\x17\xcd\xb1\x77\x5c\x31\xee\x4f\xaa\x29\x49\xe1\x00\x87\xf9\x17\x64\x21\xad\x53\x1d\xde\x01\xde\x64\xf3\x03\x7a\xf6\xb0\xf6\x78\xa1\xfc\xa4\xcf\xff\x41\xf9\x56\xd8\x5c\x88\x72\x29\x64\xfd\x77\x5c\x22\x32\x44\x35\xf1\xe9\x26\xb7\x82\xc1\xe8\x89\xd4\x44\xa3\x7b\x9a\xe8\x3c\xfd\x5f\x86\x70\x0a\x85\x84\x47\xf0\xed\xd5\x63\xed\x97\xe8\xe4\xc5\xe3\x54\x0d\xd8\xbc\x25\xd4\x1b\xa5\x15\xd2\x05\xa2\xd5\x60\xa5\x3a\xd4\x46\x43\xb9\x80\xab\x66\x4a\x6f\xd0\x27\x50\x72\xf2\xda\x9b\xf2\x6d\x8b\x6b\x52\xa0\x54\x1b\x9a\x0c\x8a\xb8\xbb\xcb\x3d\x3e\xec\x6d\x8e\xac\x88\x77\xe4\x66\x31\x6c\x25\x9f\x3f\x12\xcb\x1c\xac\xf9\x9d\x88\x0a\x2e\xa5\xa4\x09\xba\x74\x4d\x9e\x76\xf4\x9a\x05\x42\x4b\x34\x2d\xbf\x1b\x91\xe8\x1e\xd2\x26\x0e\x2a\x25\x54\x45\x68\x31\xcc\xaf\x1c\xc9\xc7\x8d\x2b\xd0\xbd\x53\x91\xb5\x8d\x71\xb8\xfe\x7a\xab\x20\x40\xa7\xa1\xc0\x4f\xce\x67\xd3\xf7\xf5\x2c\xd5\x24\x65\x3b\xaf\x6c\x72\x57\x44\x9b\x3f\xb7\x6a\x3d\x60\xc7\x3d\xce\xea\xe4\xd6\xd8\xa4\x3d\xe9\x2d\xee\xb3\x14\x64\xf5\xbb\xaa\xdb\xfd\xc2\xbb\x30\xa1\x83\xdc\x05\x92\xe9\xad\x8c\x04\xf4\x51\x25\x15\xce\xb7\xd7\x2b\x6c\x3f\xa1\x77\xc5\xf4\x5f\xbc\xd3\x28\xea\x0f\xf0\xb3\xd1\x9e\xe1\x28\x21\x06\xd9\x9b\x77\xd4\x74\x08\x12\x6f\x72\x5d\x9e\x05\x8f\xd2\x93\x72\xf4\x7c\xa1\x9a\x06\x42\xcd\xc7\xce\xc7\xaa\x19\xaf\x9a\x8b\x2c\x8e\x91\x8e\x37\x90\xa4\x36\xa9\x4b\x9b\x5a\xe8\x11\x24\xc7\xfa\x9c\xad\x74\xfc\xc4\xde\xe7\x4f\x27\x50\x90\x85\x64\xa1\xa1\xd4\x5a\xe1\x1e\x7b\x8d\x38\xd5\xcb\x01\x8e\xbc\x8c\x35\x22\xdc\x0d\x04\xcc\xe9\x4d\xe0\xb6\xba\xb5\xb2\xef\x3b\x65\x39\x90\xcb\xb5\x5d\xcc\x54\x81\x82\x28\x98\x0c\x32\xd3\x6c\x1a\x39\x35\x29\x45\x5a\x31\x91\x20\x5d\x5b\x8d\x6d\xc0\x66\xb4\x52\x6e\xf3\xad\x19\x18\x7f\x13\x16\xd2\x78\x6f\x4d\x62\xee\x0c\xa4\xc3\xc1\xf4\xba\x0f\x90\xd0\x4d\xbf\x44\x41\x5e\x86\x8e\xbe\x9e\x5f\x30\x84\x99\xf4\x55\xc5\xef\xac\x5e\x99\x46\x51\x02\x48\xe3\x77\x9b\xd6\xd2\xe7\x92\x8a\x1a\x77\x69\x03\xcb\xc1\xc9\x9f\x94\xfe\xe6\x80\xbe\x94\x89\xb3\x81\xbb\x70\x19\xc3\x5e\x68\xd2\x12\xfd\x5a\xdd\xe5\x41\xd5\xdb\x4e\x85\x02\x48\xc2\x4b\x61\xea\x44\x01\x90\x7c\x91\x7c\xfc\x86\xf6\xcd\x25\x1d\x93\x4f\xfd\xc7\xd6\xe0\xe5\xe5\xb5\x96\x52\xd9\xe3\x81\x1d\x89\x5d\x0e\x9e\xc8\xf1\x9f\x71\xdd\x2e\x91\x6b\xbd\xd3\xd3\x43\x7e\x0a\xad\x51\x59\xe5\xa9\x08\x9c\x93\xfe\x53\x7a\xdb\x8e\x47\x3d\x74\x51\x54\x6a\x0d\xc6\x28\xdd\x8d\xf2\xe1\x96\x4b\x23\x7d\x01\xae\xc7\x64\x9b\x6a\x57\xbf\xde\xe1\xcb\x36\x4c\x60\xbf\xbc\x97\x4b\xb1\x86\xb8\xcf\xf1\xdd\x77\x6d\xf2\x68\xfa\xe7\x02\x41\x00\xef\xec\xb6\x8f\x6e\xa6\x7a\x1a\x45\x85\xf2\xfb\xd9\x62\xc4\xef\x2c\xb3\x6e\xb8\x1f\x8c\x8d\xa0\xbe\x48\x45\x3f\x16\xbf\x7e\xeb\x96\xd8\x12\x63\xe9\x85\x39\x1c\xc1\xd9\x9a\x23\x99\x18\x45\x1d\x70\x3c\xf1\x7e\xb2\xe9\x28\x3f\xa2\x2f\x51\x15\x4f\x04\x32\xd8\x7a\x5c\x57\x1e\x9c\xb1\xed\x25\x09\xa5\xf3\xfb\xf7\xba\x39\x90\x54\x5e\x67\xcb\xe6\x52\x05\xee\xd9\x7d\x9a\xea\x12\xbd\xf8\xa8\x51\x33\xa3\xc9\xce\x05\x1d\x69\x50\x3f\x1a\x8d\xfb\x5f\x88\xcf\xfd\x5a\x2d\xe4\x4c\x38\xb4\x20\x79\x1c\x0f\x76\x60\x12\xdd\xa5\x31\x6d\xa5\x70\xe1\x46\xc9\xf8\xc6\x4e\xaf\x9f\xb8\x95\x91\x3d\xb2\xfe\xb5\x40\x8b\x09\x9c\x5e\xd1\x99\x60\xca\xe8\xf9\x10\xfd\x81\x7f\x05\xf8\xaf\x02\x41\x85\x6b\xec\xdc\x89\xab\xe6\x41\x14\x64\x23\x44\xb0\x95\x27\x79\xb6\xb9\x62\x65\x23\x0b\xb9\xb6\x81\xed\x47\x2a\x11\xcb\x68\x50\x50\xc0\xd8\x0d\x25\xed\xe5\xef\xf6\xab\x5e\x4e\x0f\x42\xe5\xea\xdb\xed\x31\x4d\x68\xb4\xff\xf6\x8d\xf1\x85\x0a\x04\xa5\x8d\xc1\xb5\xd4\xae\xf3\x41\xe7\x4a\xab\x3e\x77\xd3\x38\x29\xe8\x79\xde\x96\x0a\x45\xaa\xc0\x9e\x76\x08\xc9\xdb\x64\x8e\x5c\xe0\xe1\x39\x59\x88\x88\xbe\xe0\xbc\x77\x03\x99\xaa\xe3\x2e\x50\x9b\xfe\xee\xc4\xda\xc6\x32\x4d\xa8\x85\x0c\xc7\x66\xe0\x72\x66\xd9\xe8\x88\xaf\xac\x46\xb7\x28\x70\x38\x20\x87\x9c\x06\xd6\x86\x12\xc9\xd3\xf5\x35\x48\xc6\xa6\x1c\x2e\x86\x94\x4a\xb2\x11\x19\x4c\x87\xcb\xf6\x93\xe6\x0f\x58\xaa\x61\xec\xf2\xac\x19\xc1\x60\xca\x44\xb1\x9c\xc6\x91\x84\x41\x0c\xaa\x28\x31\xde\x3a\xbc\x4d\xd0\xe2\x62\x27\xa9\x1c\xe5\xe2\x8d\x4e\xdf\xa6\x5a\x69\x12\x3f\x98\x88\x2a\xe2\x57\x51\xdc\xa9\xf2\xef\x9a\xf9\xb0\xdb\x5d\x84\xec\x08\x5f\xf1\x91\x5f\xc1\x46\x92\x1a\xae\xd0\x70\x05\x93\x30\x57\xc6\xdf\x40\xb9\x5a\xc4\x67\xcf\xb0\xc6\x31\x62\x40\x3c\xfd\x4f\xc2\xcc\xfd\x9f\x2c\x3d\x27\x3f\x72\x5a\xe0\x62\x80\xe5\xfa\x32\xb2\xdc\xbc\xe4\x3b\xed\xbe\x21\xa0\x0a\x72\x4b\xc5\xc4\x77\xba\xbe\xcd\xa2\xbd\xea\x93\x66\x9b\x29\x26\x8d\x2c\x2e\x77\x9c\xac\xb0\xdb\xb7\xc3\x28\x3d\x1e\xc6\x07\x5d\x24\x0e\x2e\x35\x3a\x72\x95\x30\xcd\xcd\xe5\x44\x7f\xfa\x9a\x56\xbf\x7f\x1a\xf7\x1b\x14\xca\x87\x43\xdc\xfa\x96\x0d\x82\x65\xb6\xa9\x6e\xa3\xb8\x71\x98\x54\x28\xba\xcf\xa3\x4c\x7d\x0c\x2c\x84\x35\xb3\xef\xa8\x5c\xa3\xfb\xfa\x15\xf4\xa6\x39\x2c\x01\xbb\x87\x4a\xa2\x29\x10\x67\xbd\xe1\x92\x2a\xbc\xc5\x89\xe4\x4d\x04\x7c\x2f\x61\x3d\xbf\xd4\x4a\x79\xd8\x0b\x38\x70\xd1\x2c\x34\xbc\xb4\xf8\xb1\x36\x2e\xad\x3f\xf9\xbc\xa0\x6c\x7d\x22\xc1\xcf\x85\x15\xca\x3f\x9a\xc2\xb6\x3d\x17\x6a\xd3\x4d\xab\x34\x4e\x09\x54\xe6\x83\x03\xe9\x50\x6e\x3a\x84\x9c\x35\x0a\x45\x01\x87\x54\xc8\x1d\x9e\x1f\x6f\x08\x47\x08\xd1\x12\xd1\xba\xc8\x01\x7a\xc4\x02\xb2\xd4\x1f\x54\x91\xc1\x98\x5f\xcb\xd6\x60\x11\xff\x81\x44\x46\xc8\x5d\x21\x31\x65\xe0\xc7\xc6\x49\x13\x6b\x70\xeb\xe5\x7d\xcb\x14\x2d\xfd\x82\x2c\x5d\xa2\x7c\x0d\x1c\x75\x9b\x88\xcf\xda\xc0\x41\xc3\x44\x23\xe6\xd6\xb5\x98\x19\x60\x76\x17\x0b\x5b\x53\xd5\xd7\x0c\xa8\x6f\x4d\xd4\xda\x23\x16\xde\x7e\x1b\x84\x3b\xd0\x8e\xb9\x06\x7d\xc4\x79\x2f\xad\x1b\x59\x42\xd3\x61\x47\x83\x09\xc6\x54\x76\xa8\x3d\x67\x38\x6f\x0f\x7d\x79\x79\x1c\xd1\x8f\xbd\x41\x4c\xa2\xf1\xb8\x26\xc5\x27\xe8\x46\x48\xf4\x96\x30\x80\xc2\x8b\x0f\x53\x6c\xd6\x84\xab\x42\x9f\x4e\x5b\xab\x84\xbf\x58\x9b\x5d\xed\xee\x81\x00\xce\x08\x80\xe6\x1e\xcb\x06\x82\x89\xdd\x46\x1b\x6e\x91\xe8\x93\x9e\xfd\xef\x10\x2a\x00\x28\xe8\x03\xef\xe5\x2b\xa1\x44\xd7\xdb\x36\x05\xc5\xe4\x45\x3b\xf0\x13\x8a\x60\x70\x24\x12\xba\x69\x15\xaa\xc9\x55\x0a\x7e\x33\x3d', 2)
+## Copyright 2020-2023 Viktor Krueckl. All Rights Reserved.

+# You may obtain a copy of the License at

+# distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+# See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+# limitations under the License.
+# ==============================================================================
+
+_D='OnlyFoolsDoReadThis'
+_C='weights'
+_B='covariances'
+_A='means'
+import tensorflow as _tf,numpy as _np
+from..binning import BinningScheme
+from tensorflow.keras.layers import Layer as _Layer
+class BinYieldStatic(_Layer):
+	def __init__(A,scheme,**B):A._scheme=scheme;super(BinYieldStatic,A).__init__(**B)
+	def build(A,input_shapes):
+		B=input_shapes;A._binN=A._scheme.means.shape[0];A._sampleN=A._scheme.means.shape[1];A._outN=A._scheme.means.shape[2];A._2pi_scale=_np.power(2.*_np.pi,A._outN)
+		if A._outN!=B[_A][-1]:raise Exception(f"Distribution size ({A._outN}) does not match the integration points  ({B[_A][-1]})!")
+		A._means=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(_tf.constant(A._scheme.means.astype(A.dtype)),0),0);A._covariances=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(_tf.linalg.diag(_tf.constant(A._scheme.covariances.astype(A.dtype))),0),0);A._weights=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(_tf.constant(A._scheme.weights.astype(A.dtype)),0),0);super(BinYieldStatic,A).build(B)
+	def call(A,x,**I):C=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_A],2),2)-A._means;D=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_B],2),2)+A._covariances;E=_tf.linalg.pinv(D);F=_tf.sqrt(_tf.linalg.det(D)*A._2pi_scale);G=-.5*_tf.reduce_sum(C*_tf.linalg.matvec(E,C),4);B=_tf.exp(G)/F;B=B*A._weights*_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_C],-1),-1);H=_tf.minimum(_tf.reduce_sum(_tf.reduce_sum(B,3),1),1.,name=_D);return H
+	def compute_output_shape(A,input_shape):return input_shape[0],A._binN
+class BinYield(_Layer):
+	def __init__(A,**B):super(BinYield,A).__init__(**B)
+	def build(A,input_shapes):super(BinYield,A).build(input_shapes)
+	def call(D,x,**O):E=_tf.cast(_tf.shape(x[_A])[2],D.dtype);F=_tf.math.pow(_tf.constant(2.*_np.pi),E);G=_tf.expand_dims(x['bin_means'],1);H=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.linalg.diag(x['bin_covariances']),1);I=_tf.expand_dims(x['bin_weights'],1);B=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_A],2),2)-G;C=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_B],2),2)+H;J=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(x[_C],-1),-1);K=_tf.linalg.pinv(C);L=_tf.sqrt(_tf.linalg.det(C)*F);M=-.5*_tf.reduce_sum(B*_tf.linalg.matvec(K,B),4);A=_tf.exp(M)/L;A=A*I*J;N=_tf.minimum(_tf.reduce_sum(_tf.reduce_sum(A,3),1),1.,name=_D);return N
```

0d\xf6\xa2\xad\xce\x5a\x31\x3c\x5c\x6c\xdd\x32\x7b\x47\xaa\x36\xc0\x71\x52\x86\x79\xc5\x59\x56\x4e\x5d\x0c\xce\x19\x84\xfa\xe0\xaa\x0f\xaf\xb2\x12\x47\xf0\x7f\x31\x60\x7b\xa4\xe5\x52\xf6\x7b\x30\xd4\xf3\x49\x8e\x88\x55\x93\xbe\xe4\x3b\xab\xd1\x6c\xa6\x1e\x19\x37\x96\x3e\x0f\x60\x01\xc8\xfb\x01\xd6\x54\xa1\xa3\xa7\x6e\xe0\x26\x9e\x0d\xcd\x27\x9e\xa1\xbb\x5a\x27\x82\x2b\xd4\xb5\x61\x1f\x4b\x07\xd9\xe3\x49\x52\x15\x1f\x69\x85\x69\x62\xf6\xc6\xcb\x57\x29\xfc\x9a\x67\x4d\x2e\x74\x0a\x48\xdc\x75\x7f\x3e\x9b\xe2\xa4\xef\xbe\x61\xd0\xeb\x5c\xab\xfc\x60\x6a\x2b\xd4\xf5\x6e\x14\xb8\x08\xf8\x6d\xdc\x9b\xb1\xd9\x9d\xe8\x96\xd5\xf4\x41\xef\x3c\x3f\x9a\x2b\x78\xd9\xb1\x7b\x1f\x7e\x3f\x78\x89\x40\x42\x7a\xe6\x89\xe7\xef\x95\x8b\xbf\x81\xcb\x39\xd7\xce\x1f\x31\x35\x69\x20\xe0\x5f\x7a\xdd\x26\x13\x51\x12\xa3\xdb\x5d\x34\xa8\xe4\xa8\x80\x41\xf3\x55\xa6\xe7\x7d\x65\x1d\x2c\x19\x16\xf6\xb9\x29\xea\x16\xf5\x36\xb5\xfb\x8e\xda\x06\x2b\x09\xe9\x4a\xdf\x24\xb5\x60\xef\x6a\x51\xd2\xae\x22\xc8\xda\x61\x79\x8e\x33\x1c\xe5\x10\x81\xf8\xc4\x0b\xb3\x17\xe1\x26\x2f\x45\xf4\x07\x3a\xa0\xa1\xfe\xdf\x9a\x71\x04\xaf\x2a\x27\xfc\x14\x55\xe2\x45\xec\xe9\xc1\x62\x7b\x2a\x9b\xf2\x17\x60\xcb\x84\xef\x9a\x80\x68\x7b\x96\x47\x33\x85\x3c\xd1\x6b\x63\xca\x92\x14\x92\x31\xf6\xbc\x8e\xfa\x17\x57\x25\xe3\x8c\x14\x6c\xea\xf8\x09\xd3\x85\x86\x8e\x9d\xcf\x4f\x5a\xcf\x92\x8d\xba\xe7\xea\xd6\xd0\xd3\x2a\x9a\x76\xd5\x91\xd6\x10\xd4\xcf\x41\x0a\x10\x58\xb8\x5c\xf8\x92\x5e\x81\xa1\x2d\x6e\x97\x3b\x41\xeb\xd3\xfa\xd3\x6d\xca\x84\xf5\x57\x3d\xee\xde\x8b\xad\x22\x5c\xf5\x06\x83\x2f\xd7\x82\x19\x77\xac\xc0\x97\x9a\x3d\x0a\xc3\x09\x0e\xad\x60\x6f\x5d\xf1\x5d\x3c\x14\x93\x2b\x99\xd6\x6e\x75\x56\x87\xe3\x45\x04\x23\xbf\xe9\x33\xf2\xe7\x0c\x8f\x7b\xa8\x06\x59\x09\xff\xf5\x4e\x39\x96\xb9\xea\x18\x3d\xfe\x4e\xab\xdc\x0e\x3c\x3d\x15\xf4\x9f\x2d\x41\x6f\xdf\x4a\xf5\x90\x77\x01\xe0\xe4\xbc\x9a\xab\xfa\x43\x38\x22\x77\x96\x53\xfe\xb0\x96\xd6\x2c\xb2\xcf\xc3\x2d\xf1\x3b\xb4\x4f\x88\x76\x71\x31\xed\xeb\xb1\xfe\x78\x93\x14\x9d\xcd\x6a\x8e\x8c\xd6\x5c\x30\x17\xad\xb3\xbe\x88\x82\xc8\x17\x00\x0e\x6b\x90\x60\x9f\x46\x62\x8d\x00\xc3\x9e\xde\x4d\x1c\x3f\xc6\xc8\xd0\x49\x36\xe8\x40\xee\xf1\xfc\x0f\x77\x62\x9a\xf8\x95\xcd\x65\xa4\xef\x5a\x76\x9a\x83\x4c\x88\x36\xe3\xa8\xaf\xfa\x9b\x78\x79\x07\xf6\x77\x18\xa5\x85\x87\x74\xf9\x84\x1c\x73\xcf\x65\xa1\xe0\x41\x7d\x1c\x4b\x0c\x06\x98\x50\x6c\x2d\x8a\xab\xcf\x3f\x59\xae\x8f\xd0\x10\xf1\xa6\xce\x91\x19\x15\xc1\x68\xf5\x27\xde\xe1\x51\x07\xd9\xc6\x51\x95\x77\x85\x17\x56\xb1\x23\xab\x5d\x90\x48\x81\x1e\x5a\xa8\x69\xf9\x77\x7d\x05\xdf\x2e\x09\x8a\x75\x07\xfa\x37\x83\xb8\x2b\xa6\x20\xc9\xc3\xd4\x3f\x9d\x5c\x54\x66\xd9\xc3\x95\xfb\x4b\x68\x76\x71\xaa\x02\x63\x33\x9d\xc7\x6b\xaa\x50\x17\x3a\x5d\xbd\xc3\xfd\x94\x47\xf0\x4f\x33\x20\x37\xe1\x9c\xe1\x67\xbf\xb8\x0a\x2b\x37', 2)

+
+_C='regularize'
+_B='output_dim'
+_A=True
+import tensorflow as _tf,tensorflow_probability as _tfp
+_tfd=_tfp.distributions
+from tensorflow.keras.layers import Layer as _Layer
+from._mapping import _M
+from..distributions import createCovMatrix as _createCovMatrix
+from..distributions import regularizeCovMatrix as _r
+class TrainableCovMatrix(_Layer):
+	def __init__(A,output_dim,regularize=None,**B):A._output_dim=output_dim;A._regularize=regularize;super(TrainableCovMatrix,A).__init__(**B)
+	def build(A,input_shapes):
+		D='uniform';E=input_shapes[0];A.spread=A.add_weight(name='spread',shape=(1,A._output_dim),initializer=D,trainable=_A);C=int(A._output_dim*(A._output_dim-1)/2)
+		if C>0:A.corr=A.add_weight(name='correlation',shape=(C,),initializer=D,trainable=_A)
+		else:A.corr=[0]
+		B=_createCovMatrix(_tf.exp(A.spread),_tf.tanh(A.corr),A._output_dim)
+		if A._regularize:B=_r(B,A._regularize)
+		A.matrix=B;super(TrainableCovMatrix,A).build(E)
+	def call(A,x,**C):B=_tf.shape(x)[0];return _tf.tile(A.matrix,[B,1,1])
+	def compute_output_shape(A,input_shape):return input_shape[0],A._output_dim,A._output_dim
+	def get_config(A):B=super().get_config().copy();B.update({_B:A._output_dim,_C:A._regularize});return B
+class VarCovMatrix(_M):
+	def __init__(A,output_dim,regularize=None,**C):B=output_dim;A._output_dim=B;A._regularize=regularize;super(VarCovMatrix,A).__init__(output_dim=B,**C)
+	def build(A,input_shapes):
+		B='normal';D=input_shapes[0];A.spread_mean=A.add_weight(name='spread_mean',shape=(A._output_dim,),initializer=B,trainable=_A);A.spread_std=A.add_weight(name='spread_std',shape=(A._output_dim,),initializer=B,trainable=_A);A.spread=_tfd.Normal(A.spread_mean,_tf.exp(A.spread_std));C=int(A._output_dim*(A._output_dim-1)/2)
+		if C>0:A.corr=A.add_weight(name='correlation_mean',shape=(C,),initializer=B,trainable=_A)
+		else:A.corr=[0]
+		super(VarCovMatrix,A).build(D)
+	def call(A,x,**F):
+		C=_tf.shape(x)[0];D=_tf.cond(A.sampling,lambda:_tf.exp(A.spread.sample(C)),lambda:_tf.expand_dims(_tf.exp(A.spread_mean),0));E=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.tanh(A.corr),0);B=_createCovMatrix(D,E,A._output_dim)
+		if A._regularize:B=_r(B,A._regularize)
+		A.matrix=B;return B
+	def compute_output_shape(A,input_shape):return input_shape[0],A._output_dim,A._output_dim
+	def get_config(A):B=super().get_config().copy();B.update({_B:A._output_dim,_C:A._regularize});return B
```

ce\xe8\xab\x8d\x08\x35\x22\x7b\x0b\xc5\x34\xa7\x78\x3f\x37\x29\x90\x81\xef\x9e\x70\x12\xb9\x65\xc2\x5f\x88\x9c\x63\xb0\x4c\xd3\x67\x3f\x65\x89\x24\x0d\xfb\x5b\x0c\x0a\xce\xc6\x2c\x24\xc3\xec\xd5\xb0\xc4\x84\x4c\x08\xfa\x28\x13\xeb\xe8\x27\x3c\xfb\xb7\x70\x1e\x84\x1a\xf3\xb3\x12\xa7\x8b\x7d\xa6\x37\x65\xe0\xdc\xa8\x75\xe5\x1e\x61\x88\xc9\x9a\x14\x91\x65\x35\xf0\xa2\x3a\x1e\x01\x0a\x7d\xf0\x78\x07\x75\x47\xc0\x8c\xb2\x67\x6c\x0e\x54\x53\x11\xc6\x7c\xa4\x55\xda\xd7\x21\xae\xd1\x70\x36\x15\x35\x1f\xd2\x70\xf1\x84\x18\xac\x8a\xa9\x02\xbe\x37\x48\x50\x00\x7e\x59\xa4\x40\x02\x63\x47\x37\x43\xd3\x2c\xaf\x98\x12\x69\x1d\xe4\x47\x39\x7a\x3e\x0c\x1d\xfc\x2e\x28\xfe\x97\x69\x80\x6f\xe3\x69\x5c\x11\x24\x7e\x6c\xa5\x3a\xc8\x41\x7f\x3c\xf5\x43\x16\xa4\xf5\x71\x13\x99\x1c\x9b\xa3\x5e\x2c\xf1\x33\x3d\x9c\xa0\x4e\x32\xdc\x57\x37\x5b\xe7\x69\xc6\x25\x02\xe9\x31\xfd\xf2\x82\xfe\x06\xea\x91\x36\x4c\xf1\xfd\x70\x28\x0d\xdd\xd4\x11\xff\x5c\x7e\x6a\x62\x06\x4f\xe2\xfb\xfe\x5b\xfa\x48\x85\xc5\x4b\xa0\x31\x27\xcb\x67\xda\xe3\x75\x52\xad\x15\x44\xf8\x9d\xc6\x1d\x69\x09\x81\xba\x96\x8f\x12\x7c\x09\x2c\xab\xfb\xeb\xd8\xaa\x96\x07\xd6\x95\x11\x54\xf4\x60\xf6\xdf\xdd\xaa\x5b\x45\xef\x03\x03\x66\xf4\x92\xf5\xe3\x0f\xfe\x0f\x6a\xa6\x11\x31\xed\x5e\x7f\xae\x30\x5c\x24\xfe\x44\x05\xa4\x88\xab\xdd\xd3\xb5\x7c\x32\xec\xee\x87\x26\xef\xf9\x3e\x0a\xe6\x5f\x0f\x7c\x00\xc0\xa9\x1b\x29\x9b\x36\xf7\xc3\x81\x20\xd7\xc0\x58\x79\x97\xc0\x1d\x22\xe0\xa7\x1b\x18\xa1\xe1\x4c\xe8\x2a\xcb\x84\x3c\x0e\x33\x11\xd3\x46\xda\x5e\xf5\xf0\x7b\xb9\xd8\x23\x3f\x42\x61\x4b\x8e\x49\x58\x09\xdd\x23\x29\x23\x0b\xa8\x10\xba\x8c\xd6\x89\x02\x5b\x5c\x49\x66\x9b\x7e\xf0\x7c\x2c\x52\x13\xaa\x8c\xb2\x03\xad\xcc\x91\x89\x78\x8f\xef\x80\xce\x25\x8f\xba\x81\x8c\x3a\x6c\xcd\xe5\xd0\x41\xda\xf0\xcd\x25\x64\x2b\x00\xa9\x80\x24\xfd\x2f\x89\xc9\xa6\x82\xa6\x0a\x3a\xbc\x68\xb1\x31\x6a\x6a\x04\x2c\x09\xc4\x5a\x04\xcc\x1e\xf2\x7f\xf3\x83\x79\x81\xa3\xf8\x28\x87\x14\x06\x8a\xb0\x98\xc7\xdb\xa8\xab\x1a\x3c\xc4\xa9\xff\x3a\xd4\x0a\xe9\x81\xcc\xc4\xf9\x24\x23\x90\x4f\x24\x35\xa0\x18\x46\x6c\x29\x0b\x23\x6d\x37\xf3\xc9\x11\xf7\xf0\x93\x8e\x05\x23\x70\x6e\xef\x75\x92\xee\x2e\x75\xda\x3a\xbe\x32\x1b\xf2\xff\x15\x95\x88\x69\x04\x1a\xb5\x88\x67\x6b\x53\x36\xcf\xa2\x1a\x0a\x4a\x38\x20\xb7\x8d\x69\x4d\x63\x8d\x82\xd2\x9c\xd8\x18\xf2\xad\x72\x39\x49\x76\x35\x59\x97\x29\xf1\x79\x91\xa9\x95\x9c\x97\xab\x34\xdf\xe1\x55\x73\x5f\x71\xfe\x81\x43\x0e\xf8\xa4\x3c\xf6\x5f\x3d\x90\x8c\x47\x8f\x63\x53\x0e\xa7\xdf\xe4\xfb\x7c\xb0\x2a\x21\x3a\x0c\x11\x7e\xdb\x17\xd0\xeb\xcc\x5f\x31\xb8\x16\x2d\x2a\x05\x49\xdb\x0c\x20\x8d\xcd\xeb\xb9\x6e\x94\x12\x7b\xae\x80\x6d\x10\xd8\x1e\x86\xcc\xe7\x64\x1b\xd0\x54\x62\x7c\x7d\xaf\xfd\x33\xa5\xb8\x53\xa4\xa7\x89\x2e\xcd\x50\x6a\x88\xb7\xc7\xb4\x61\x0d\xaa\xde\x90\x6d\xe0\x34\xe2\x31\x97\x92\x87\xf8\x23\xc5\x7d\xbb\x8c\x47\x74\xac\x34\xe1\x7d\x6b\x65\x8f\xe2\xb8\xa9\xae\x19\xc2\x4e\x23\x0f\x87\xf9\x90\x3c\x4b\x3b\x96\x70\xc2\xe8\x34\x69\x46\xea\x57\x54\xb6\xab\x4c\xf4\xbc\x1b\x45\x15\x97\xe1\x39\x96\xc8\xc7\xbe\x09\x64\xb3\x43\x68\x88\xc1\xd9\x61\x2f\x94\xda\xd7\x1d\x99\x8d\x40\xdb\x13\xb3\x4d\xf3\xe0\xe6\x80\x94\x6b\xaa\x3d\x8a\xe2\x7e\xc0\x43\x23\x0f\x0a\x7b\xdb\xd1\x30\x28\x12\x1a\xaa\xe2\xeb\x38\x26\x84\xd0\x38\x92\x35\x82\x2c\x9b\x46\xce\xf8\x7f\x28\xe2\x6b\x2e\x53\x03\xcc\xd0\x50\x48\xb2\x68\x1b\x33\x52\xd4\xc4\x69\x51\xc6\x6a\xfa\x73\x49\x3f\xc0\xc1\x25\xbf\x19\x9d\xfb\x0d\x63\x0c\x4a\xc9\x2c\x79\xad\x5f\xe6\x40\x12\x54\x37\xa4\x20\xcd\x16\xf0\x26\xeb\x14\x6c\x04\xa2\xfe\xbe\xe9\xfe\xe7\xae\xc1\x4d\x49\x2c\x62\x72\x99\x2c\x09\xbd\x31\xa8\x11\x9b\x80\x25\x16\x57\x24\x39\x65\x87\xd9\x73\x61\x9d\xf9\x22\xe0\xb2\xbe\xda\x1a\x33\x84\x09\x2b\xd3\xf3\xa4\x90\x86\x53\x3a\x58\x31\x25\x7c\xbc\x40\x69\x09\xfb\xce\x24\xc9\xeb\x4e\x30\xae\xd6\x74\x14\x61\xe1\x50\xab\xa2\x6d\x65\x98\x86\x6c\x17\x4d\xf8\xe6\xa8\xe1\x16\xd0\x6f\x95\xcc\x5b\x60\x43\xad\x56\x3d\x42\x73\x36\x31\xcb\xdb\x37\x0a\xfd\x46\x3a\x09\xba\x89\x88\x6a\x90\x8e\xbd\xdd\x18\xc5\x09\x32\xcb\xd7\xaf\x80\xc9\x08\xd2\x1a\xe8\xdc\x8c\x9d\x83\xc4\xaf\x36\x8b\x4d\xc0\x5a\x0b\x2d\x84\xb4\x2c\x66\x51\x18\x96\x9f\x77\x92\x42\xea\x6b\xfb\xca\xa7\x0b\x84\x9d\x80\xd5\xc5\x40\x79\x6f\xab\xb5\xcb\x10\xd0\x0b\xc2\xbc\xfb\x03\x62\xab\xc6\xfa\x6e\x32\xfd\x3d\xb5\x0d\xa0\x05\xf9\x01\xd0\xab\xd1\xbe\x2f\xfb\x03\x42\x3e\x9c\xad\x18\x1d\x0b\xce\x36\x07\x39\x65\x46\x8a\xc7\x19\x7b\x65\xa3\x83\x41\x23\xd2\xd3\x35\xac\xb6\xe9\xd8\xae\x88\x52\xa2\x2a\x24\x53\xf7\xf7\x82\x5d\xee\x1f\x17\x0c\x9e\xf9\x91\x9d\xfa\x40\x4b\x1b\x35\x9d\xc5\xb8\xa0\x61\x10\xd1\x54\x56\x71\xc4\xda\xfb\xd8\x8d\x66\x70\xcf\x2f\xc6\x83\x7a\xca\xe9\x37\xd9\x8d\xaa\x38\x1f\x00\x73\xdb\x09\x1e\x4e\xb5\x51\xed\xa5\xee\x54\x72\x85\x28\x48\xcd\x8d\xdb\x30\xc1\xb3\x7c\xe3\x9f\x36\xa8\x7e\x4f\xbd\xee\x8f\xb2\x68\xbb\xbc\xdf\xe5\x8d\xde\x90\x85\xbc\xd4\xc6\x93\x2c\xea\xfb\x9f\x67\xa0\x7d\xe6\xe0\x08\x7c\x0a\x0e\xe1\xf6\xc8\x30\xd9\x66\xae\x33\x7d\x86\xcd\x48\x38\x85\x3e\xa1\xfa\x74\xdd\xc4\x53\xf3\x7a\x50\x3f\xda\x34\x2c\x73\xa7\x1b\xc8\xdc\x54\x56\xfa\x16\xce\x41\x9c\x31\x38\xec\x58\x7f\x74\x1f\xab\x4a\x3d\xad\x40\xfb\x43\x41\x0a\x35\x13\x36\x41\xca\x69\x11\xb7\x47\xc1\xea\xd0\xfa\x53\x25\x60\x99\xd9\xcf\x05\x36\x10\x17\xbd\x74\x79\x96\xff\xdd\x06\xa0\xe7\xc5\x81\xbe\x87\xe2\x50\x6d\x48\x1a\x37\x9f\xeb\x4a\xc4\xae\xe8\x84\x2e\xc0\x7a\xa5\xaf\x25\xd3\xdf\x88\x57\x08\x10\xb5\x10\x4b\xcb\x2f\xc8\xf5\xfa\xc4\xc7\x49\x97\xc6\x0d\x96\xf8\x6f\x7c\x04\x14\x5a\xb7\x08\xfc\x60\xff\xa6\x13\xe2\x4e\x73\x35\xea\xe9\x81\x57\xa0\x63\x87\x7f\x4e\x4e\x45\x4c\x19\x71\xd8\xe5\x42\xac\x03\xac\x38\xa4\x53\xdd\xb8\x09\x98\x0c\x53\xe6\xe4\x76\xa5\xc9\x48\x54\xda\x81\x36\x77\x3c\x66\xc5\x73\xad\xda\xdf\xc3\xc4\x62\xaa\xb2\xc6\x51\x9d\x94\xd8\x09\xac\x7e\x05\x75\x48\xa2\xa8\x69\x34\x89\x78\x24\x24\xad\xd5\x6c\xc3\x26\xf2\xfa\x71\x37\x4c\x33\xeb\x5b\x3f\x70\xaf\x06\x15\x34\x1f\x50\xe3\x58\x49\x7d\xf5\x58\x58\x7a\xeb\xe3\x6f\xa3\x90\x29\x1c\x9c\x12\xef\xe2\x48\xa5\xb6\x57\xed\x2b\x0e\x0f\x33\x33\x3e\x6f\xd7\x53\xb7\xfd\x49\x1a\x6b\x21\xf8\x5a\xbf\x86\x16\x9d\xc4\x9b\x7a\x3e\x65\xf0\xdd\x e7\x2f\x00\xc7\xb7\x29\xb4\x9f\x33\x30\x63\xd8\xfb\xda\x9a\xa7\xe0\x83\xc5\xc9\xa9\x71\x50\xf8\xc3\xfc\x2c\x84\x6a\x33\xc9\xbb\xb0\xa8\x2d\x62\x1d\x18\x99\x19\x9c\x34\xbe\xd0\x98\xd1\xb5\x56\x08\xbd\xae\x46\x42\x9b\xe0\xd2\x47\x83\x86\x86\x5b\x9c\x50\x7b\xe7\x7c\xb1\xd4\x48\x0a\x18\x5e\xfc\x67\xed\x7a\xad\xd1\x1d\xc8\x1b\x2f\x85\x93\x04\xe0\x9e\x08\xd6\x0c\x69\x08\xc0\xbd\x44\x6e\xef\x18\x72\x5e\x04\xae\xde\x47\x12\xb0\xc4\xaa\x9c\x2a\xc8\x37\x08\x89\xd0\xe7\x72\x6a\x78\x3c\xcd\x8c\xe0\x3a\x72\xf1\xf7\xd5\xce\x47\x3c\x29\xbe\xae\x4b\x69\xb8\x37\x68\xac\x3a\x21\xe5\x08\x38\xf9\x53\xed\x2e\x64\x97\x8a\xd1\xfb\xed\x4d\x77\xc1\xe4\x35\xfd\x49\x5f\x38\x78\x34\x5c\xf2\x2e\xc5\x56\xce\x0c\x11\xcf\xa1\xf6\x7f\xad\xfd\x20\x2a\x6e\x55\x0b\x29\xea\x66\x23\x55\x67\x9a\x58\x7e\x1f\xf2\x2a\x8c\xc8\xe2\xc1\x82\x49\x2d\xa7\x8e\x93\xf0\x5d\x61\x88\x52\xf5\x5c\xd8\x0f\x44\x96\x58\x79\xd6\x20\xa8\x35\x68\xf4\x3f\xd3\xdb\xb1\x31\xc3\x6d\x25\x60\xad\x05\x92\xb9\xdc\xd1\xd3\x97\x5c\xe7\xe6\x62\x77\x7d\x0c\xbe\x06\xf0\x5c\xa1\x1f\x1b\x39\x9f\x21\xc1\x77\x9d\x16\xf2\xdf\xb2\xd2\x2b\xfc\xa2\x34\xe7\x2c\x16\x5a\xa8\x4b\x86\x43\xd4\x02\x68\xfa\x6d\x25\x2e\xef\x52\x28\xa0\xee\x3d\x5a\x52\xf1\x7d\x47\xd2\xc2\xd5\x17\xee\x42\x27\x2b\x0b\x28\x03\x12\x5b\x29\x73\xfa\xc8\x17\xd3\xdc\x4d\xad\x86\x77\x7f\x2b\xbe\x30\xc4\xa8\x12\x28\x5b\x5f\xf9\x99\xa0\x5c\x2f\x30\x59\x76\xc4\x87\x3f\x9e\x01\xd8\xc9\x52\x60\x13\x6f\x45\x4f\xf4\xa9\x83\xef\xd8\x92\x25\x94\x64\xcd\x19\x13\x0d\x43\x81\x05\xdd\xf4\x44\xce\x7d\x11\x75\x45\x7b\xd0\x2a\x95\xf3\xb5\xec\xfc\x35\x9b\x8f\x84\x62\xe2\x47\xdf\xe0\xb5\x05\x1b\x45\xac\x32\x18\x66\x0c\xe5\xba\x82\xa9\x38\x56\xf2\xce\x6e\xe3\x9f\xab\x7a\x1a\x11\xe8\xd8\x3c\x68\x95\xc1\x43\x53\xcb\xf0\xa2\xcb\x56\x44\x6e\xd9\xe7\x63\x00\x91\x64\xec\x73\xe1\xc9\x34\x65\x62\xc2\x30\x31\xe8\x22\xcd\x93\x15\xe6\x39\xe4\xb2\xb5\xc8\x5c\x26\x8c\x6b\x6d\xf9\xb3\xf5\xd4\x9b\x1f\x94\x92\xe2\x98\x86\x00\xf8\x22\x00\xd4\x8d\x2c\xd8\x48\x97\xb0\x60\xf0\xd2\xaa\xb7\xbe\xb3\xc4\x71\x6c\x7b\x73\x64\x
