a9\xdd\x0d\x18\xc2\x5a\xb8\x96\x88\xa1\xcc\xe0\xe3\x61\x6d\x79\x96\x5e\x9b\x57\xa1\x76\x95\x02\xf6\xf6\x36\xf0\x7b\xe3\x04\x56\x19\x3d\x62\x5a\x0e\x1b\x0f\x5f\x66\x4a\x94\x60\x02\x92\x11\xf3\x9d\x7a\x79\x73\xd7\xe9\x0d\x47\xa7\x89\xef\x10\xdd\x59\x66\x80\x73\xd3\xf0\xc9\xce\xc2\xe9\x9c\xb7\xb9\x8c\x81\x7a\x3c\xfa\x5a\xa5\xd8\xda\x97\xd1\x02\x9d\x3c\xbd\x97\x30\x9c\x8b\x1f\x11\xaa\x75\x8d\xe1\xd1\xb1\x3c\x20\x36\x5c\x36\x5f\xf8\x22\xef\x72\xef\xc8\x4d\x38\x2c\x41\x59\x68\x29\x35\x34\xbb\x15\x0f\x09\x61\xd7\xb4\xa0\x73\x16\x47\xa7\x9e\x34\x04\x20\x2f\x7c\x0d\x31\x8d\x5e\x62\x5e\x47\x70\x2f\x84\xcc\x07\x97\x1b\xce\xb3\x31\x87\x5d\x61\x99\x20\x93\x5f\xac\x7d\xd3\x17\x5a\x25\xf0\xbb\x91\x65\xdf\xd6\x00\x9e\x85\x5d\xb0\x1c\x18\xf0\xb3\x5b\x3e\xc0\x34\x6f\x88\xc3\x85\x5e\x60\x06\x73\x59\xb4\x0e\x59\x13\xf9\x31\x75\xda\x45\xeb\xaf\x80\xca\x53\x24\xbf\x5a\x6a\x76\x0e\xbf\xc6\xfb\xc4\x36\x15\x7a\x17\x85\xa2\x3c\xeb\x62\x8c\x27\x8e\x6b\x6c\x28\x99\x48\x27\x2d\xa5\x32\xed\xf6\x86\xc1\xad\x54\x31\x1d\xf2\x60\x7c\xee\xba\x7d\xed\xc5\x2d\x8a\xd6\x78\xbe\x86\x12\x1f\x27\x6a\x66\xc0\x10\xdf\x42\x89\xed\x71\xfa\x50\x36\x07\xea\xcf\x65\x99\xb1\x2b\x84\x6f\x11\x1b\xfb\xf6\x2e\x4d\x8e\xb7\x4f\xa1\x34\x41\x84\x45\x02\x09\x4d\x41\x57\xbf\x44\xc1\x90\x92\x2a\x3d\x95\x00\x6b\x4e\x0b\xa3\x06\xf9\xee\x84\xdc\x7d\xcd\x41\x62\xcd\x92\xb4\xee\x32\x72\x3e\x71\x0b\x98\xec\xed\xf1\x47\x61\x06\xa8\x74\x0e\x3d\xbc\xb0\xda\x6e\x3a\x85\x35\x51\x8f\x73\x3e\x4d\xc2\x77\xa8\xbf\x79\x6e\x83\x88\xbd\x94\x24\xaf\xe0\x7f\x43\xd3\x22\x6c\x7c\xe6\x9a\x3c\x46\xfc\x09\x77\xce\x7b\x26\x6d\x6a\xf0\x59\xf4\xd7\xbf\xd1\x83\x98\x56\xc5\x4f\x33\xa0\x99\xab\x56\x2a\x02\x20\x8a\xdf\x87\xe7\x51\x0d\xf1\x26\x9c\xf4\x76\x21\xf6\x85\x4d\x12\x21\xf4\x93\xb8\x4a\xf2\xc6\x49\xca\xd7\xdf\x09\x0b\x78\x07\x16\xb3\xfc\x6d\x46\xc3\x2d\x55\x6d\xaa\xf9\x9c\xeb\xa4\x15\xfe\x96\xbc\x19\xfe\x43\x5b\xc0\x5a\x97\x46\xd4\x29\x47\x34\x70\x86\x51\x24\xd0\x6f\xba\x39\xec\xb3\x1c\xa8\x21\xbb\x8a\x5c\x33\x52\x55\x62\xfd\x34\x11\x07\x6a\x2c\x27\x c4\x10\xab\x3b\x54\xe3\xb1\xa7\x8a\xab\x7e\xaf\xd7\x84\xf0\x76\x27\x44\x47\x45\xc3\x32\x8d\x4c\x17\x4c\x2b\x2d\x8c\xd3\x87\x86\x38\xc4\x21\xd1\x4a\x14\xeb\x6a\x6b\xfd\x00\x3a\x39\x0a\xe9\xaa\x29\x1b\xf0\xd3\x82\x3c\x87\xb9\xa2\x63\x15\x00\xcd\xa4\x08\x01\x03\xd4\x89\x17\x2f\x88\x4f\x29\xe4\x00\xd8\x6a\xcb\xaa\xd9\x7f\xb9\x6a\xde\x1f\x50\x59\x5c\xa5\x81\xd7\xaf\xad\x07\x67\xd3\xd6\xbc\x4f\xaf\xe7\x90\x8b\x3d\x2d\x2b\xb5\x62\x87\x57\x0f\x82\xaf\x31\xcc\xed\xb6\xe3\x2f\x3b\x5a\x63\xdd\x40\xcc\x84\xf8\x38\xcf\xd6\x27\xe0\x71\xb0\x0e\x93\x19\xfb\xf7\x08\x24\x5d\x3e\x56\x00\xbd\x71\x9b\x5c\x78\x21\x90\x19\x0f\x75\x8e\x64\xe8\x4f\x10\x20\x28\x31\x96\xd7\xc4\x16\x4c\x52\x96\xfe\xc5\x75\x03\xd4\x7c\xcb\xa2\xf8\xba\xd0\xb4\x96\x8a\x0e\x99\x17\x3c\x6b\xbc\x3e\x37\xa4\x5d\x86\xe7\xb4\xcf\x58\x6f\x3e\x10\x05\x9f\xbf\xd3\xf7\x38\x4b\x5f\x19\x35\x85\x4a\x99\xc8\x59\x88\xfc\x2d\x1c\x77\x3d\x37\x60\xff\x1b\x2a\xff\xd2\x11\x06\xde\xa5\x83\x1e\x3a\x0a\xb5\x4d\x17\x34\x36\x8d\xb7\x53\x8e\x03\x5d\x03\x63\x52\xf3\x51\x96\x9f\x16\x51\xe0\x95\x4f\xa6\x74\xcb\x75\x87\x3c\xfa\xff\xb2\x63\xe6\x93\x29\x5f\x72\x8d\x6b\xce\x01\x19\x3f\x7e\x39\xec\xa4\x6a\x5b\x29\x5e\xc2\x27\x7d\x3b\x6d\x83\x15\x65\x8e\x8d\x3a\x5e\xd6\x1f\x2e\x67\x4d\x99\x58\x95\xee\xe3\x88\x06\xeb\xb8\x3e\xf8\xbb\x25\x7f\x0d\x40\x84\xc3\x0b\x7f\x62\x6a\xbc\xa5\xf3\x0c\x8e\x6f\xa5\x5d\xd6\x59\x5e\x55\x55\x56\x44\x17\xc4\xdd\x61\x36\xaa\xf6\x67\xd9\x06\x33\xf0\xfe\xe5\x2b\x83\xcf\xf9\x68\x2d\x66\x62\x0a\x3c\x15\xea\x40\x73\x97\xf2\xa8\x45\xf8\x50\x9c\x22\x3f\xd0\xf2\x4d\x54\xa1\xc4\x49\x2a\x0b\x60\x22\xeb\x11\x77\x01\x3a\x03\x77\xa2\x78\x75\xe5\x81\xef\xe7\x48\x0d\x6d\xa6\xfa\x8f\x03\x0e\xf0\x0e\x5b\x2c\x75\x0b\x25\xa3\x47\x0c\xc4\xd9\x81\x86\x43\xbc\x45\x22\x1c\x5d\x5c\xa3\xb3\x57\xd1\x30\x75\x62\x67\x84\x3a\xb5\x63\xef\x28\x3d\x57\xb5\x07\x6d\x14\x63\xa3\x2a\x81\x4c\xca\xed\x52\xc5\xb4\xcb\x7a\x88\xd8\x8c\x42\xe9\xab\x1d\x2c\x4a\xfe\x5d\xb7\x55\xdc\x2a\x84\xb6\xf5\xfa\x78\x15\x12\x30\xee\xd0\x6a\x42\xf8\x85\xd8\x6a\x4c\xca\x98\x 69\xd5\x13\x6c\x0e\x09\x74\x2d\x8f\x8f\xa0\xfd\xcf\xec\xc6\xa8\x12\x0b\xa7\x03\x9b\x85\xa0\xf0\x2a\x83\x9a\x2e\xa9\xc2\x3b\x0c\x44\x1a\x86\x45\x25\x7c\xba\xcf\x97\x1a\x74\x83\xf9\x80\x8e\x55\xfa\x00\x36\x0e\xae\x78\x8b\xb1\x79\x6a\x0a\x20\x52\xf2\x11\x5d\xe3\x93\xdd\x4c\xe0\x82\x08\x00\x0a\xbf\x3b\xa0\x0e\x01\xa8\xaf\x48\xf4\xa8\x9e\xd0\x4b\xc8\x45\xb2\xa7\x12\xa8\x2b\xa7\xc3\x7e\x4b\xde\xe5\xa6\xb1\x0a\x0f\xb3\x49\xc3\x6f\x23\x87\x53\xa0\xdf\x4f\x92\x95\x19\x58\x50\x9c\xe2\xb6\xd8\x7d\x79\x06\xb3\x86\x53\x22\x69\x54\xd3\x64\x56\x86\x29\x48\xec\x11\x93\xff\x87\x70\xd8\x7d\xb4\xc8\x3f\x6b\x57\xdc\xc1\x1e\x99\x89\x68\x9d\x6a\x48\xb4\x19\xc3\xfb\x49\xee\x58\x8f\x3d\xcb\x56\xc9\x9a\xda\x25\xc7\x6e\x65\x83\xd8\xb9\x50\x1e\xc2\x70\xf8\x5c\xdd\xdf\x5a\x5e\x6a\x06\xb8\xe6\xbe\xf2\x26\xdd\xf9\x8e\xeb\xcf\x3c\x75\xfd\x1d\x4a\xb8\x90\x52\xcf\x57\x7c\xe6\xa9\x9b\x8c\x67\x69\xdc\xd6\x14\xf0\x78\x8c\xb2\x63\xa2\x09\x51\xcc\x05\x67\x51\x91\xb8\xaf\xab\xdf\xec\xc1\x09\xbc\xab\x8a\x21\x6d\xb0\x1a\xba\x6f\xe7\xad\xce\x91\xe7\x16\x7b\x20\x7e\x2a\x0e\x1a\xd0\x0d\x12\x90\x8a\x98\xbf\xfc\x67\x29\x93\x9a\x65\x81\x66\xaa\x08\x3d\xe1\x88\xaf\xcd\x95\xdc\x88\x54\x2c\xc8\x0e\xcd\xeb\xbd\x6f\x65\x14\x1e\x6f\xe8\x7d\x51\xa3\xbf\xb2\xef\x59\x9c\x1e\x13\x34\xa3\x28\x93\x94\xbf\xd5\x89\x7f\x0a\x61\xd5\x23\xab\xbf\xb5\xc9\x10\x38\x09\x11\xb3\x97\xc7\x56\xa3\x1a\xde\xbe\x7a\x54\x45\xc1\xeb\xee\x46\xb5\x0b\x88\x03\x4d\x6d\x69\x62\xe1\x5e\xeb\xd7\x2a\x05\x9d\xb2\xc3\x04\x38\x7d\x52\x44\xc8\x37\x49\x36\xbd\x88\x8d\x2b\xf0\x60\x10\x95\xc5\x6f\x12\xd0\x71\xcc\x8d\x78\xf4\x60\x09\x53\x27\xcb\x7f\x00\xba\xaf\x1a\xbc\x59\xe3\x4e\x89\x16\xd2\x81\x54\x69\x3d\x22\x81\x9a\x13\xca\x53\xb2\xb3\xba\x09\x47\x2c\x47\x01\xdc\x4d\xb6\x91\x3e\x28\x5e\xdd\x7d\xd8\x94\x33\xd6\x04\xd8\xde\xf7\x02\x2f\xb2\xe0\x9a\x4c\x5f\x2f\xfd\xf0\x97\x67\xc0\x31\x47\x30\x9d\x91\xbe\x3e\xf8\xd4\xd8\xa5\xf8\x10\xfc\x16', 2)
```diff
+## Copyright 2020-2023 Viktor Krueckl. All Rights Reserved.
+#
+# Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+# you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+# You may obtain a copy of the License at
+#
+#     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0

+# limitations under the License.
+# ==============================================================================
+
+_B='weights'
+_A='means'
+import tensorflow as _tf,tensorflow_probability as _tfp
+_tfd=_tfp.distributions
+from._mapping import _M
+from..distributions import regularizeCovMatrix as _r
+class LinearMapping(_M):
+	def build(A,input_shapes):
+		D=True;C='normal';B=input_shapes
+		if not(_A in B and _B in B):raise Exception('means and weights are needed to construct the mapping layer!')
+		A.mix_dim=B[_A][1];A.input_dim=B[_A][2];A.kernel_mean=A.add_weight(name='kernel_mean',shape=(A.input_dim,A.output_dim),initializer=C,trainable=D);A.kernel_std=A.add_weight(name='kernel_std',shape=(A.input_dim,A.output_dim),initializer=C,trainable=D);A.bias_mean=A.add_weight(name='bias_mean',shape=(A.output_dim,),initializer=C,trainable=D);A.bias_std=A.add_weight(name='bias_std',shape=(A.output_dim,),initializer=C,trainable=D);A.kernel=_tfd.Normal(A.kernel_mean,_tf.exp(A.kernel_std));A.bias=_tfd.Normal(A.bias_mean,_tf.exp(A.bias_std));super(LinearMapping,A).build(B[_A])
+	def call(A,x,**M):
+		I='covariances';H='stdDevs';D='covB';C='covA';F=_tf.shape(x[_A])[0];J=_tf.cond(A.sampling,lambda:_tf.matmul(x[_A],A.kernel.sample(F))+_tf.expand_dims(A.bias.sample(F),1),lambda:_tf.matmul(x[_A],A.kernel_mean)+A.bias_mean);G=_tf.expand_dims(_tf.expand_dims(_tf.stop_gradient(A.kernel_mean),0),0)
+		if H in x:K=_tf.transpose(_tf.expand_dims(x[H],2),[0,1,3,2]);E=_tf.multiply(K,G)
+		else:L=_tf.linalg.sqrtm(x[I]);E=_tf.matmul(L,G)
+		A.mappingCov=_tf.matmul(_tf.transpose(E,[0,1,3,2]),E);B=A.mappingCov
+		if C in x:
+			if len(x[C].shape.dims)==3:B=B+_tf.expand_dims(x[C],1)
+			else:B=B+x[C]
+		if D in x:
+			if len(x[D].shape.dims)==3:B=B+_tf.expand_dims(x[D],1)
+			else:B=B+x[D]
+		if A._regularize_cov_epsilon:A.covMatrix=_r(B,A._regularize_cov_epsilon)
+		else:A.covMatrix=B
+		return{_A:J,I:A.covMatrix,_B:x[_B]}
```
